Ntibibaho k’umugabo yemeye Imana yiwe y’ukuri canke k’umukenyezi yemeye Imana yiwe y’ukuri hamwe n’intumwa yiwe mugihe baciriwe urubanza babe bafise aho bahengamiye kuri urwo rubanza rwabo, nuwu hakana Imana mu kwiyonkora ku Mana hamwe n’intumwa yiwe, mu vy’ukuri uyo muntu azoba yazimiye bimwe biri k’umugaragaro
Igihe yabwira umwe Imana yahaye imigisha yiwe uca uramu hezagira, nufate umutambukanyi wawe kandi utinye Imana yawe, nukunyegeza ibiri kumutima wawe mugihe Imana yawe ariyo nyene ukuri nuguca utinya abantu aho gutinya Imana yawe y’ukuri mugihe uyo Zaidi yarangiza amabanga yiwe nkenerwa, nuyo mupfasoni niho twamuha uburenganzira bwukubakana nuyo mupfasoni kugira ngo ntihabe imyikeko n’ingorane kuba Isilamu mu kwubaka izabo n’abana babo b’abazanano mugihe bataba keneye, n’itegeko ry’Imana niryo ritegerezwa gukurikizwa gusa
Ntamwikomo kuntumwa y’Imana kubintu Imana imaze kumu menyesha, bikaba ari ibisanzwe ku Mana ku bantu bahise baho hambere n’itegeko ry’Imana n’iteguro riteguwe neza
Abahora bashikiriza ubutumwa bw’Imana hamwe nukuyitinya, rero ntanuwo batinya atari Imana, n’Imana niyo ihagije muguharura
Intumwa y’Imana Muhammadi (aui) si umuvyeyi y’uwariwe wese muba shingantahe banyu, ahubwo n’intumwa y’Imana yanyuma muntumwa zayo zose, n’Imana niyo ifise ubumenyi bw’ibintu vyose
Mwebwe mwemeye Imana yanyu y’ukuri, ni mwibuke Imana yanyu kenshi na kenshi
Kandi muyihayagize iyo Mana kuva mugitondo no kumugoroba
Niyo ibaha iyo migisha hamwe n’Abamarayika biwe kugira ngo ibakure mumwijima nukuba shikana mumuco, kandi niyo iha imigisha yayo cane aba Isilamu
Indamutso zabo zo k’umusi w’ihuriro n’Imana zizoba arindamutso z’amahoro, kandi yabateguriye impembo z’iteka ntangere
Ewe ntumwa y’Imana, mu vy’ukuri twebwe twakurungitse ngo utubere icabona cugutanga inkuru nziza nukuba mu bantu batuza
Kandi ube mu bantu bararika abandi kubera Imana, kandi kw’itegeko ryiwe, kandi ube uri urumuri rutanga umuco
Kandi ubahe aba Isilamu inkuru nziza yuko bafise akarusho kaniniya kavuye ku Mana yabo
Ntugamburukire abo bahakanyi b’Imana hamwe nabo babeshi, kandi ntiwiteho kumabi yabo, mugabo ugume wizera Imana yawe gusa, kuko ariyo ihagije mukugu kingira
Mwebwe mwemeye Imana yanyu y’ukuri, ni mwubakane n’abakenyezi bemeye Imana yabo y’ukuri hanyuma ni mwahukana nabo batambukanyi banyu imbere yuguhuza nabo ibitsina, ntavyicaro bafise muzoba harurirako, mugabo nimubahe ico mwoba shumbusha kandi muze mwahukane nabo munzira nziza z’amahoro
Ewe ntumwa y’Imana, twaraguhaye uburenganzira kubatambukanyi bawe wahaye agashimwe kabo hamwe nabo witungiye mukuboko kwawe kw’iburyo, wahawe n’Imana yawe hamwe n’abigeme babadata banyu batoyi, hamwe n’abigeme bayinasenge banyu, n’abigeme bayinarume banyu, n’abigeme babashiki banyokwanyu mwimukanye nabo, hamwe n’umukenyezi wumu Isilamukazi yitanze kubwiwe imbere y’intumwa y’Imana, nkuko intumwa y’Imana nawe yagomba kwubakana nawe kandi berekuriwe kuriwe gusa bitarekuriwe kubandi ba Isilamu, ntankeka twebwe turamaze kubimenyesha ivyo twabategetse kubakenyezi babo hamwe n’abakenyezi mwitungiye kumaboko yanyu y’iburyo kugira ngo ntihabe ingorane kuri wewe, n’Imana niyo nyene imbabazi nyinshi n’impuhwe zihagije
Usubiza inyuma kuwo wishakiye muribo, nukwegereza hafi kuwo wishakiye, niwaba wamugomye uwo wamaze kwahukana nawe sibibi kuri wewe kugira gutyo kuzotuma unezereza amaso yabo aho kugumana agahinda kandi bashime wabahaye uko bari kwose, n’Imana niyo ifise ubumenyi bw’ibiri mumitima yanyu, kandi niyo ifise ubumenyi, kandi niyo ntungane
Munyuma yaba bapfasoni ufise ntabundi burenganzira ufise bwukubaka n’abandi bakenyezi canke kubahindura n’abandi bakenyezi naho ubwiza bwabo bwokunezereza dukuyemwo mubo wintungiye k’ukuboko kwawe kw’iburyo, n’Imana niyo irereka ibintu vyose
Mwebwe mwemeye Imana yanyu y’ukuri, ntimwinjire mumazu y’intumwa y’Imana kugeza aho muhabwa uruhusha rwukuja gufungura, nukutarindira kugeza aho ivyo bifungurwa bihira, mugabo ni mwaba mufise ubutumire aho niho murekuriwe kwinjira, kandi muhejeje gufungura nimuce mwitahira mutarinze gushinga ibiyago kuko ibintu nk’ivyo vyamye bishavuza intumwa y’Imana, nawe aho ari akagira isoni, mugabo Imana ntibona isoni ivugishije ukuri, namwe mugihe mubajije abapfasoni biwe nimubabarize inyuma y’uruzitiro, kugira gutyo n’ugusukura imitima yanyu hamwe n’imitima yabo, kandi sivyiza gushavuza intumwa y’Imana canke kwubakana n’abapfasoni biwe munyuma yiwe, rero kugira gutyo kizoba ari igicumuro kininiya cane imbere y’Imana
Nimwa serura icarico cose canke mukaki nyegeza, ntimuzi yuko Imana ifise ubumenyi bw’ibintu vyose
Ntagicumuro kuribo no kuri badata babo, canke kubibondo vyabo, canke bene wabo, canke kubana babene babo, canke abana babashiki babo, canke abakenyezi nkabo, canke bamwe bitungiwe n’amaboko yabo y’iburyo, nimutinye Imana yanyu mwebwe bakenyezi kuko ntankeka Imana niyo cabona kiri hejuru y’ibintu vyose
Mu vy’ukuri Imana imanura imigisha kuntumwa yayo hamwe no kuba marayika bayo, rero mwebwe aba Isilamu kandi muyisengere intumwa y’Imana muyisabira amahoro y’Imana n’imigisha nukumusabira amahoro
Mu vy’ukuri bamwe bashavuza Imana hamwe n’intumwa yayo, abo bantu Imana yarabavumye kuri iy’Isi no mw’ijuru, kandi yaraba teguriye ibihano bibatetereza
Nabarya bashavuza abagabo baba Isilamu hamwe n’abakenyezi babo ata n’ikosa narimwe bagize, ntankeka abo bantu nabikoreye ubuhemu buniniya hamwe n’ibicumuro biri k’umugaragaro
Ewe ntumwa y’Imana, niwongorere abakenyezi bawe, hamwe n’abigeme bawe, hamwe n’abakenyezi baba Isilamu bamanure neza impuzu zabo, bagize gutyo bizotuma bamenyekana kugira ngo ntaba girirwe inabi, n’Imana niyo ifise imbabazi nyinshi n’impuhwe zihagije
Niba abo babeshi hamwe nabafise ingwara mumitima yabo hamwe n’abiyamamaza kumabi yabo bari mugisagara, mu vy’ukuri twebwe tuzobigukura ko hejuru yabo hanyuma ntibazo kwicara ngaho hafi yawe atari mumwanya mugufiya gusa
Abo bantu baravumwe aho bari hose naho babonekera hose nibafatwe kandi bicwe
Ibi nibisanzwe kumana kuvyabayeho kubantu bamyeho kera, kandi ntuzoronka ihindagurika ry’ibintu bisanzwe ku Mana
Abantu bakubaza inkuru z’umusi w’umuhero w’isi, wewe nuvuge uti:- ubwo bumenyi buri ku Mana yonyene gusa, none n’igiki kizo kumenyesha ko nkumbure umusi w’umuhero w’Isi uri hafi yugushika
Mu vy’ukuri Imana yarabavumye abahakanyi bayo, kandi yaraba teguriye umuriro udahera
Bazowuguma mwo mubuzima bwabo bwose, kandi ntibazo ronka umukunzi canke umufasha
N’umusi waho mumaso yabo hazohinda gurirwa mumuriro udahera baze bavuge bati:- iyo tugamburukira Imana hamwe nuku gamburukira intumwa yiwe Muhammadi (aui)
Bazovuga bati:- Muremyi wacu, mu vy’ukuri twebwe twakurikiye abategetsi bacu hamwe n’abakuru bacu, abo rero nibo batuzimije munzira y’ukuri
Muremyi wacu, nubahe ibihano bimwe vy’akarorero abo bantu, vy’incuro zibiri zibiri, uteko ubavume umuvumo muniniya
Mwebwe mwemeye Imana yanyu y’ukuri, ntimube nkabagoye intumwa y’Imana Mussa (iii) mugabo Imana imugira mweranda kuvyo bamuvuzeko, nawe akaba yari afise urupfasoni ntangere imbere y’Imana
Mwebwe mwemeye Imana yanyu y’ukuri, nimuyitinye Imana yanyu y’ukuri, kandi muvuge amajambo y’ukuri
Izobagirira ibikorwa vyanyu vyiza, kandi izobagirira imbabazi kubicumuro vyanyu, nuwu gamburukira Imana hamwe n’intumwa yiwe, ntankeka uyo muntu azoba afise intsinzi niniya cane
Mu vy’ukuri twebwe twaraseruye amategeko yacu hamwe n’amatuzo yacu, kumajuru yose hamwe n’Isi n’Imisozi, vyose vyarahakanye kwakira ayo mategeko nukuyatinya, mugabo umuntu yarayakiye, ntankeka umuntu niwe muhemu mukuru, kandi atabwenge afise
Kugira ngo Imana ihane abagabo b’ababeshi n’abakenyezi bababeshi hamwe n’abagabo bagereranya Imana n’ibindi bintu, hamwe n’abakenyezi bagereranya Imana n’ibindi bintu hanyuma ize igirire ikigongwe aba Isilamu b’abagabo n’abakenyezi, n’Imana niyo nyene ikigongwe cinshi n’impuhwe zihagije
Nidukengurukire Imana, kuko nivyiwe ibiri mu Majuru no kw’Isi no k’umusi w’imperuka ihayagizwa ryiza niryiwe, kandi niyo nyene ubuhizi n’ubumenyi buhagije
Niyo ifise ubumenyi bw’ivyinjira kw’Isi hamwe nibiva muriyo hamwe n’ibishunguruka bivuye mw’Ijuru hamwe n’ibiduga muriyo nayo niyo nyene ikigongwe cinshi n’impuhwe zihagije
Abahakanye Imana yabo y’ukuri baravuze bati:- uwo musi w’umuhero w’Isi twebwe ntuzo dushikira, wewe nuvuge uti:- nukubera iki? K’ukuri k’Umuremyi wanje ntankeka uwo musi uzobashikira kuwufise ubumenyi bw’amabanga yose ntakizo kwinyegeza n’ikintu nakimwe naho coba gifise uburemere bw’akanyegeri kari mw’Ijuru canke kw’Isi canke ikintu gitoyi gisumba ico canke kininiya gusumba ico, nuko vyose biri mugitabu kibitomora neza kandi kiri k’umugaragaro
Ize ibarihe bamwe bayemeye bimwe vy’ukuri nukugira ibikorwa vyiza, abo bantu nibo bazoronswa ikigongwe n’imigisha y’iteka
Nabihanganye muguhakana aya majambo yacu y’ukuri bagaca babona yuko bazodutsinda, abo bantu bazoronka ibihano bibi kandi bibabaza cane
Nabahawe ubumenyi barazi neza yuko ivyamanuwe kuri wewe bivuye kumuremyi wawe arivyo vy’ukuri nayo irongora munzira y’uwufise ubushobozi kandi ininahazwa hose
Nayo abahakanye Imana yabo y’ukuri bavuze bati:- mbega tubamenyeshe umuntu ababwira yuko mugihe muzota bagurwa mukaba ibimanyu manyu yuko muzoba muri murindi remwa rishasha
Mbega yariyadukije n’ububeshi hejuru y’Imana canke n’umusazi, ahubwo abatemera umusi wimperuka nibo bazoba bari mubihano no mubuzimire bwakure cane
Mbega ntibabona ibiri imbere yabo hamwe n’ibiri inyuma yabo biri mw’Ijuru no kw’Isi, rero iyo dushaka twari kubahonya kuri iy’Isi canke twari kumanura hejuru yabo ibimanyu vy’amajuru, ntankeka muri ibi vyose harimwo itekerezo k’umuntu uwariwe wese yigaruye ku Muremyi wiwe
Mu vy’ukuri twarahaye intumwa y’Imana Daudi (iii) imigisha mininiya ivuye kuri twebwe tuvuga duti:- mwamisozi mwe, nimwitabire muri kumwe nawe mugu takambira hamwe n’inyoni zose, duca tumworohereza icuma
Nuhingure inkinzo zagutse, kandi uzipime neza mukuzunga, kandi mugire n’ibikorwa vyiza, ntankeka ndabona ibikorwa vyanyu vyose mugira
No kuntumwa y’Imana Suleimanu (iii) twaramu gamburukije umuyaga w’urugendo rwo mugitondo rwafata ukwezi kumwe n’urundi rugendo rwo kumugoroba narwone rwafata ukundi kwezi kumwe, duca tumu shuhiriza isoko ry’ubutare bw’umujumpu, no mubisigo vyagize ibikorwa imbere yiwe kw’itegeko ry’Umuremyi wiwe, nuwiyonkoye kw’itegeko ryacu muribo twaca tumu honjesha ibihano vy’umuriro waka cane
Bahora bamugirira imirimo y’ivyo ashaka vyose haba munzitiro n’amasanamu hamwe n’ibirindi bininiya bingana nk’aho bakarabira hamwe n’amasufuriya maniniya cane adashoboka kuva aho yashizwe, rero nimukore mwa bantu b’intumwa y’Imana ya Daudi (iii) mugushimira imigisha Imana yabahaye, kandi nimu bantu bakeyi cane bashima mu bantu banje
Mugihe yasandaba ntamuntu n’umwe yabamenyesheje kuri urwo rupfu rwiwe atari umuswa wariye inkoni yiwe, rero mugihe yarwa hasi niho ibisigo vyamenya yuko iyo bamenya ayo mabanga y’urwo rupfu rwiwe ntibari kwicarira muri ivyo bihano bitetereza gutyo
Ntankeka ico cari icirwa ku bantu bokwa Saba’a mungo zabo no mumirima y’impande zibiri kuruhande rw’iburyo no kuruhande rw’ibubamfu, hose nimufungure kuri iyo migisha y’Umuremyi wanyu kandi muyi kengurukire n’iki gisagara ciza, n’Umuremyi wawe afise ikigongwe cinshi gihagije
Mugabo ntibitayeho kumategeko y’Imana rero twaciye tuba shungurira ishunguriro rininiya ry’amazi ryatumye tubahindurira imirima yabo n’iyindi mirima ibiri harimwo ivyamwa bifise akanovera gakaze cane hamwe nayarura, n’ibindi navyo nka Ath’lin hamwe na Sid’rin n’ibindi
Uku niko twahaye indishi yabo kubera ubuhakanyi bwabo natwe ntitubahana atari k’umuntu yahakanye Imana yiwe y’ukuri
No hagati muribo hamwe no hagati y’ibisagara twahezagiye hamwe n’ibindi bisagara vyaboneka twashizemwo ibituro vy’ingenzi tubabwira duti:- nimubigendere ijoro n’umutaga muri mumwidegemvyo w’amahoro
Mugabo bavuze bati:- Muremyi wacu, nutugirire urugendo rurerure ruri hagati y’ingendo zacu zose, nabo baca bahemukira imitima yabo ari naho twabacirako umugani nukuba shwiragiza kure nakure, mu vy’ukuri muri ivyo vyose harimwo icirwa ku bantu bigumya nugushimira Imana yabo y’ukuri
Ntankeka wamwansi w’abantu bose ariwe yitiriwe Ibilisi yaremeje amakenga yayo ari hejuru yabo nabo baca baramu kurikira dukuyemwo umurwi wabemera Imana yabo y’ukuri
Nawe ntabubasha yari ifise kuribo mugabo kubera yuko twagomba kwerekana uwariwe muribo yemera umusi w’imperuka n’uwufise amakenga, n’Umuremyi wawe niwe aziganya ibintu vyose
Vuga uti:- nimu hamagare abo babemerera izindi Mana atari Imana y’ukuri zidafise n’uburemere bw’agakoko gafise n’uburemere bungana n’akanyegeri koba kari mw’ijuru canke kw’Isi, kandi ntaho bacuditse muri ivyo vyose, kandi ntamufasha ifise muribo
Kandi ntikuzo fasha ugusabirwa kwabo imbere y’Imana atari kuri wa muntu yahawe uruhusha kugeza naho hakurwamwo ubwoba buri mumitima yabo niho bazovuga bati: Umuremyi wacu yavuze iki? Nabo bazokwishura bati:- Yavumereye ukuri nayo niyo iri hejuru y’ibintu vyose kandi niyo nkuru
Vuga uti:- ni nde abaha imigisha ivuye mw’Ijuru no kw’Isi ? Na wewe nubishure uti:- n’Imana yonyene, kandi ntankeka twebwe canke mwebwe, turi hejuru y’uburongozi canke turi mubuzimire buri k’umugaragaro
Vuga uti:- mwebwe ntimuzo bazwa kubicumuro twebwe twagize kandi twebwe ntituzo bazwa kuvyo mwebwe mugira
Vuga uti:- Umuremyi wacu niwe azo twegeranya twese hanyuma aze aducire urubanza rw’ukuri ruzoba hagati yacu nawe niwe mucamanza afise ubumenyi bukwiye
Vuga uti:- nimunyereke uwabahujije n’Imana ngo mube mubafasha biwe, ivyo rero ntibishoboka mugabo niyo yonyene Mana ifise ubushobozi n’ubuhizi buhagije
Ntitwakurungitse atari ku bantu bose, kandi ube umutanzi w’inkuru nziza hamwe n’uwutuza, mugabo abantu benshi ntavyo bazi
Nabo bavuga bati:- niryari hazoba iri sango nimwaba muvugisha ukuri
Vuga uti:- murafise isango ry’umusi mutazo cerezwa kuriryo sango n’isaha n’imwe canke mutazo yitanguriza imbere y’igihe cayo
Baravuze b’abahakanyi b’Imana yabo y’ukuri bati:- twebwe ntituzo kwemera iyi Qur’aani namba canke ivyo bindi bitabu vyabayeho imbere y’ico gitabu, rero iyo wobabonye abo bahemukiye imitima yabo bahagaritswe imbere y’Umuremyi wabo nabo baterana imirarwe y’amajambo kuribo n’abandi, bamwe banyarucari bazobabwira bamwe bishima nukwibona mubakuru babo bati:- iyo hataba mwebwe ntankeka twari kuba aba Isilamu b’ukuri
Bazovuga bamwe bishima mubakuru babo bababwira bamwe banyarucari bati:- yo! twebwe twarabazitiriye uburokoke munyuma yaho bwabashikira, ahubwo mwebwe nyene mwari mu bantu babi cane
Nabamwe banyarucari bazovuga bababwira bamwe bishima aribo bakuru babo bati:- ahubwo amarorerwa mwagira y’ijoro n’umutaga mugihe mwadutegeka ngo duhakane Imana nukuyigira ngo tuyigirire abafasha bayo nabo bazonyegeza agahinda kabo bafise mugihe bazobona ibihano vyacu, natwe tuzoshira iminyororo mumazosi kuri bamwe bahakanye Umuremyi wabo w’ukuri, none hari ibindi bintu barihwa atari muvyo bahora bagira
Rero natwe ntitwarungitse umuntu abatuza muri ivyo bisagara ivyarivyo vyose atari kubasangwa baho bifitiye uburyo bavuze bati:- ntankeka twebwe turiyamirije n’ibi mwarungikanywe navyo
Nabo babishura bati:- twebwe turafise amatungo menshi hamwe n’ibibondo vyinshi kandi natwe ntituzohanwa
Vuga uti:- mu vy’ukuri Umuremyi wanje yama yugururira imigisha kuwo yishakiye nukwima kuwo yishakiye mugabo abantu benshi ntavyo bazi
Si amatungo yanyu canke ibibondo vyanyu bizobegereza iwacu kurugero rwo mw’ijuru, ahubwo uwemeye Imana yiwe y’ukuri hamwe nukugira ibikorwa vyiza abo rero nibo bazoronswa impembo niniya cane kubera ibikorwa vyiza bakoze, nabo bazoba bari mumahoro ntangere kandi bari mumazu agerekeranye kuyandi ari mw’Ijuru
Nabamwe bihangana muguhakana amajambo yacu bakabona yuko bazodutsinda, abo rero nibo bazoshengezwa mubihano
Vuga uti- mu vy’ukuri Umuremyi wanje yugururira imigisha yayo kuwo yishakiye ku bantu bayo kandi ikima kuwo yishakiye, n’icarico cose muzotanga niyo izobariha nayo niyo nyeranda yabatanga iyo migisha
N’umusi Imana izo begeranya abantu bose hanyuma ize ibwire Abamarayika bayo iti:- mbega aba bantu bamye babasenga mwebwe
Nabo bazokwishura bavuga bati:- uri kure n’ibida kwiranye na wewe, kandi ni wewe mukunzi wacu, sabo gusa ahubwo bamye basenga ibisigo na benshi muribo barabemeye
Kuri uno musi benshi muribo ntibazo shobora bamwe muri mwebwe kubaha agahengwe bagenzi babo canke kuba kuriraho ingorane barimwo, kandi tuzobabwira bamwe bahemukiye imitima yabo duti:- ni muhonje ibihano vyo mumuriro udahera mwamwye muhakana
N’igihe basomewe aya majambo y’Imana matagatifu yacu ari k’umugaragaro baca bavuga bati:- ntiyari kuba uyo Muhammadi (aui) atari uko ari umuntu ashaka kuba kingira hamwe nivyo bahora basenga abavyeyi banyu, nabo bishura bati:- ntivyari kuba ibi vyose atari ububeshi bwadutse giturumbuka, n’abahakanye Imana y’ukuri babwira ukuri kwabashikiye bati:- ibi vyose ntivyari kuba atari uko ari uburozi buri k’umugaragaro
Kandi ntitwa bahaye ibitabu ngo babisome kandi ntitwa barungikiye uwuba tuza imbere yawe
Barahakanye bamwe bamye imbere yabo kandi ntibara ronka ahantu hica cumi civyo twabahaye kuko baciye bahakana intumwa z’Imana zanje, rero ibihano vyanje vyari bimeze gute kuribo
Vuga uti:- jewe ndiko ndabakebura kw’ijambo rimwe gusa, yuko mwohagarara bwuma kubera Imana muri babiri babiri canke umwe umwe hanyuma muce mwiyumvira muvuge muti:- uyu mwene wanyu si umusazi, rero ntiyari kuba atari uwuba tuza imbere yuko hashika ibihano bikaze cane
Vuga uti:- impembo nabasavye nirwanyu mwebwe ntampembo yanje atari kumana yanje gusa nayo niyo cabona c’ibintu vyose
Vuga uti:- ntankeka Umuremyi wanje niwe akwiragiza ukuri, akaba ariwe nyene ubumenyi bw’ivyo twebwe tutazi
Vuga uti:- ukuri kwashitse, n’ikinyoma ntikizozana ikindi kintu gishasha, kandi ntikizo shobora gusubiza inguvu zaco
Vuga uti:- ninaba narazimiye ntakundi, nzoba narazimiye kubera yuko nacumuriye umutima wanje wonyene, ninaba nara rongotse nukubera yuko nahawe ubutumire buvuye ku Mana, n’Umuremyi wanje ntankeka niwe yumva kandi niwe ari hafi
Wokwirabira ingene bahahamutse mugihe bazobona ibihano vy’Imana babe nk’abashaka kwiruka mugabo ntamahungiro azoba ahari kuko bazofatwa mumwanya mugufiya kandi hafi cane kandi barashika na kure
Nabo bazo vuga bati:- ubu rero turayemeye mugabo bazo shobora kuronka gute ubwo bw’Isilamu bari mukibanza ca kure
Mugihe bari bamaze kwidohora kuva kera kandi bakaba batitayeho kumajambo ataboneka avuye ku Mana nayo bayataye ahantu hakure
Hazoshirwaho uruzitiro ruzoba ruri hagati yabo no hagati y’ivyo bipfuza nkuko bagiriwe bagenzi babo baho hambere, ntankeka rero abo n’abantu bari bafise amakenga yatumye binubana kubera idini rya Isilamu
Nidu kengurukire Imana Umuremyi w’Amajuru n’Isi, kandi ikaba ariyo yagize Abamarayika kuba arizo ntumwa zifise amababa abirabiri n’atatatatu hamwe n’anane, ikaba yongereza mukurema kwayo uko yishakiye, ntankeka Imana niyo nyene ubushobozi buri hejuru y’ibintu vyose
Imigisha Imana yugurura kubantu bayo, ntawushobora kuyikingira, kandi ntawu shobora kuyegeza imbere, nayo niyo nyene ubushobozi n’ubuhizi buhagije
Mwebwe bantu, nimwibuke imigisha y’Imana iri hejuru yanyu mbega hoba hari uwundi muremyi atari Imana yonyene gusa ibaha iyo migisha ivuye mw’Ijuru no kw’Isi, rero ntayindi Mana isengwa bimwe vy’ukuri atariyo yonyene gusa, none ni hehe muhindukizwa
Niba baguhakana umenye yuko bahakanye intumwa z’Imana imbere yawe n’ibintu vyose bizosubizwa kumana
Mwebwe bantu, ntankeka isango ry’Imana niry’ukuri, rero ntimuhendwe nubu buzima bwo ng’aha kw’Isi canke wamubeshi mukuru yitiriwe Ibilisi ntabahende kubera Imana yanyu
Mu vy’ukuri Shetani n’umwansi wanyu, namwe rero nimu mugire umwansi wanyu, kuko ihamagarira umurwi wayo kugira ngo ube ari uwo murwi wo mumuriro udahera
Abahakanye Imana yabo y’ukuri hazoba kuribo ibihano bikaze cane, nayo abemeye Imana yabo y’ukuri nu kugira ibikorwa vyiza, abo bantu nibo bazoronswa ikigongwe hamwe n’impembo itagira uko ingana
Mbega umwe basharije ibikorwa vyiwe bibi, nawe akabibona yuko ari vyiza, ntankeka Imana yama ireka umuntu yishakiye akazimira, nukurongora uwo yishakiye, rero umutima wawe ntukuvemwo kubera agahinda kuribo, mu vy’ukuri Imana niyo ifise ubumenyi bw’ivyo bagira vyose
Imana niyo isunika imiyaga, ikana yinyarutsa hamwe n’ibicu ikabi shikana kw’Isi yapfuye, no kuriyo tugaca tunagisha iyosi mugihe yari yarapfuye, nivyaba ari uko niko kuzurwa kwanyu
Uwushaka ubutegetsi, nuko ubwo butegetsi bwose ari ubw’Imana gusa, iwe niho haduga amajambo meza, n’igikorwa ciza nico kiduza amajambo amajambo meza gusa, nabamwe bagira ingeso z’amarorerwa mabi mabi, abo nibo bantu bazoronka ibihano bikaze cane, n’ingeso mbi zabo bantu zizohonywa
N’Imana niyo yabaremye ibakuye mw’ivu, hanyuma kw’ima ry’intanga, hanyuma ibagirira abagabo n’abagore, n’umugore uwariwe wese ntashobora gusama imbanyi canke ntiyibaruka atari kubumenyi bw’Imana, nuwahawe ubuzima ntahabwa ubwo buzima bw’umurengero canke ntagaba nirizwa kuri ubwo buzima atari uko vyose biri mugitabu c’Imana gitagatifu, ntankeka ibi vyose biroroshe imbere y’Imana
N’ibiyaga bibiri ntibimeze kumwe n’ikindi, kuko kimwe gifise amazi apfuse y’umusarara amanuka neza mumuhogo, n’ayandi nayo nay’umunyu abishe, no muri ivyo biyaga niho mufungura mwo inyama nshasha nugukura mwo ibisharizo mwambara, no muri ivyo biyaga mubonerayo amato asatura amazi kugira ngo muronkere mwo akamaro kayo kandi muteko muyishimire
Niyo yinjiza ijoro mumutaga, nukwinjiza umutaga mw’Ijoro hanyuma igira Izuba n’Ukwezi, ivyo vyose bigenda ijoro n’umutaga kugeza k’umwanya wagenewe ushike, iyo niyo Mana, Umuremyi wanyu nyene ubwami, nabarya bayisenga ukutariko abo ntanico batunze nigishishwa c’urutete rw’umutende
Nimwabasaba ntibumva akamo kanyu naho bokwumva ntiba shobora kubishura, no k’umusi w’imperuka bazohakana ubwo bugereranyi bwanyu bw’Imana y’ukuri, kandi ntibazo kubwira yuko bari hafi y’uwufise ubumenyi bw’ukuri
Mwebwe bantu, ni mwebwe muri abakene kumana, nayo Imana niyo nyene ubutunzi kandi niyo ininahazwa hose
Ibishatse yoba kuraho mwese nukuzana ibindi biremwa bishasha
Ibi vyose ntibigoye ku Mana
Ntawuzo kwikorera itu ry’uwundi muntu nuwoba yatakariwe n’iryo tu ryiwe, ahamagaye mugenziwe kubera iryo tu ryiwe, ntawuzo ryakira na gatoyi naho yoba ari mugenzi wiwe, mu vy’ukuri urabatuza kuri barya batinya Umuremyi wabo mugihe batamubona nugu hagarika amasengesho yabo, nuwisukuye yisukura kubera umutima wiwe n’ingaruka y’ibiremwa vyose ni ku Mana yonyene gusa
Ntibangana impumyi hamwe n’umuntu abona
Canke umwijima hamwe n’umuco
Canke igitutu n’ubushuhe
Kandi ntibangana abahema n’abapfuye, mu vy’ukuri Imana irumvisha uwo yishakiye, mugabo wewe ntushobora kwumvisha abari muntatemwa zabo
Ntiyari kuba wewe atari uko uri umutuza gusa
Ntankeka twebwe twakurungitse kubera ukuri kwama kugira ngo ubashikirize ubutumwa bw’Imana uteko ubatuze, kandi nt’abantu kw’Isi abaribo bose bataciyeko n’uwuba tuza
Nibaguhakana naho, umenye yuko bahakanywe n’abari imbere yabo kuko bashikiwe n’intumwa zabo z’Imana bakaba nabo baje bafise ivyemezo biri k’umugaragaro hamwe n’ibitabu vyukwandikira ko hamwe n’ibitabu birimwo umuco
Hanyuma narabafashe bamwe bahakana Imana yabo y’ukuri, rero ibihano vyanje vyari bimeze gute
Mbega ntubona yuko Imana yamanuye amazi avuye mubicu, no kuriyo twakuyemwo ivyamwa bifise amabara atandukanye n’ayandi, no kumisozi harimwo n’imirongo yera niy’itukura ifise amabara atandukanye n’iyindi yirabura cane
No mubantu hamwe no mubikoko harimwo murivyo vyamvura, n’ibindi bikoko bifise amabara atandukanye, mu vy’ukuri mubatinya Imana yabo bimwe vy’ukuri mu bantu biwe nibarya bafise ubumenyi, ntankeka rero Imana niyo nyene ubushobozi n’imbabazi zihagije
Mu vy’ukuri bamwe basoma igitabu c’Imana gitagatifu ca Qur’aani nugu hagarika amasengesho yose no muvyo twabahaye bagatanga mumwiherero no k’umugaragaro abo nibo bizeye ibidandazwa bidahomba
Kugira ngo ibahe impembo yabo ikwiye nukubongereza inyungu zayo, mu vy’ukuri niyo nyene ikigongwe nugu shimirwa
N’igitabu twagu shikirije dukoresheje ubutumwa bw’Imana, nico gitabu c’ukuri cemeza ivyabaye imbere yiwe, ntankeka. Imana kubiremwa vyayo niyo ibazi kandi niyo ibabona
Hanyuma twabasigiye ibisigi vy’iki gitabu gitagatifu ca Qur’aani mu bantu twatoye mu bantu bacu beranda rero muribo harimwo abahemukiye imitima yabo, n’abandi babayabaye, hakaba n’abandi bagenda imbere mukugira ibikorwa vyiza kw’itegeko ry’Imana, iyo rero niyo migisha mininiya
Imirima y’ubudahera bazo kwinjira mwo, muriyo bazo sharizwa n’imigufu vy’inzahabu hamwe n’ibisharizo vyo mumazi bitiriye (ilulu), n’impuzu zabo zizoba zihwahutse cane
Bazovuga bati:- ama ninahazwa yose meza na y’Imana yadukuyeko agahinda, mu vy’ukuri Umuremyi wacu niwe nyene ikigongwe cinshi na nyene gushimirwa
Niyo yaturekuriye inyubakwa yukubamwo mubuzima bwacu bwose, muri iyo nzu ntavyago birimwo canke uburuhe
Nayo abahakanye Imana yabo y’ukuri, bazoba bafise umuriro udahera witiriwe Jahannamu, ntibazo ciribwa urubanza rw’ugupfa, kandi ntibazo gabanirizwa ivyo bihano, uku rero niko duhemba abadashima
No muri uyo muriro udahera bazokoma yo induru muri uyo muriro udahera bavuga bati:- Muremyi wacu, dukure muri uyu muriro udahera tugire ibikorwa vyiza bitameze nk’ivyo twahora tugira tukiri kw’Isi, mbega ntitwabahaye ubuzima bw’ukwibuka uwibuka, nugushikirwa nuwutuza, rero nimuhonje ibihano mwebwe mwahemukiye imitima yanyu kuko mudafise uwuzoba rokora
Mu vy’ukuri Imana niyo nyene ubumemyi bw’amabanga y’ibiri mu Majuru no kw’Isi ntankeka rero Imana niyo nyene ubumenyi bw’ibiri mubikiriza vyacu vyose
Imana niyo yabagize ngo mube ivyegera vy’abandi kuri iy’Isi, rero uko guhakana kwiwe kuri kugatwe kiwe n’ubuhakanyi bwabatemera Imana y’ukuri ntaco zibongereza imbere y’Umuremyi wabo atari ugushavurirwa gusa n’ubwo buhakanyi bw’abatemera Imana ntaco bubongereza atari uruhombo gusa
Vuga uti:- mbega murabona abo mucuditse nabo aribo musenga aho gusenga Imana y’ukuri, rero nimu nyereke n’ahantu hatoyi h’Isi baremye canke boba bafise ishirahamwe mu Majuru canke twarabahaye igitabu no kurico bakaba bagifitiye ko ivyemezo biri k’umugaragaro, mugabo abahemukiye imitima yabo ntibapfundika amasezerano yabo atari uko arimwo ibinyoma gusa
Mu vy’ukuri Imana niyo ikingiye Amajuru n’Isi kugira ngo ntaveho, kuko avuyeho ntanumwe yoya kingira atariyo yonyene gusa, ntankeka rero Imana niyo ntungane n’ikigongwe cinshi gihagije
Bararahiye ku Mana indahiro yabo niniya bavuga bati:- niba shikirwa n’uwubatuza ntankeka bazoba mubazo rongoka gusumba abandi bantu, mugabo mugihe bazoshikirwa n’uwuba tuza ntaco yobongereje atari uguhakana uko kuri gusa
Kubera amanyama yabo kuri iy’Isi nukugira akajagari kabi kabi, nako kajagari kabi kabi ntikamanuka atari kuri beneko bakagize, none hari ikindi barorereye atari urutonde rwamyeho no ku bantu baho hambere, kandi ntuzoronka ihindagurika ry’urwo rutonde rusanzwe rw’Imana yagenye, canke ntuzosanga ihindagurika riri mubintu bisanzwe vy’Imana
Mbega ntibagize urugendo kuri iy’Isi bakibonera impera n’imperuka yaba bayeho imbere yabo, kandi bakaba bari abantu bafise ubushobozi kubasumba, kandi ntakindi kintu gishobora kunanira Imana haba mw’Ijuru canke ng’aha kw’Isi, ntankeka rero Imana niyo ifise uburemyi n’ubushobozi bukwiye
Iyo Imana ihana abantu kubera ivyo bakoze ntiyari gusiga n’umuntu numwe ngaha kuri iy’Isi canke n’igikoko na kimwe, mugabo Imana niyo iba rorereza kugeza k’umusi wagenywe, rero igihe c’umusi wabo kizoshika mu vy’ukuri Imana ku bantu bayo niyo ibabona
Ya, Siiyn, (Insiguro y’izi ndome hamwe nuwufise ubumenyi bwazo bwose n’Imana yonyene gusa)
Ndarahiye kuri aya majambo y’Imana matagatifu ya Qur’aani yateguwe neza cane
Yuko mu vy’ukuri wewe uri muntumwa z’Imana
Uri hejuru y’inzira igororotse
Nimanurwa ryanyene ubushobozi n’impuhwe zihagije
Kugira ngo ubatuze abantu batatujijwe n’abavyeyi babo, rero nibo babaye abasamajwe
Ntankeka n’ijambo ryemejwe kuri benshi muribo, kuri ivyo rero ntibavyemera
Mu vy’ukuri twebwe twashize iminyororo kumazosi yabo kugeza kubusakanwa bwabo, rero imitwe yabo iraramye iri hejuru
Twashize imbere yabo uruzitiro ruri imbere yabo n’urundi ruzitiro ruri inyuma yabo duca tubafuka mumaso yabo kuribo, kuri ivyo rero ntibabona na gatoyi
Nivyiza kuribo ubakebuye canke utabakebuye ntibazokwemera
Woshobora kumutuza urya akurikira ubutumwa bw’Imana yamara kunyurwa nayo majambo y’Imana agaca atinya nyene imigisha naho atayibona rero numubwire uyo yuko ikigongwe hamwe n’impuhwe z’iteka ziri kuriwe
Mu vy’ukuri twebwe tuzozura abapfuye kandi twandike ibikorwa vyabo bagira ntibize bisigare inyuma, n’ibintu vyose biri mububiko bw’igitabu cerekana ibintu vyose
Nubagirire akarorero k’abantu bo mugisagara kanaka mugihe bashikirwa naba shikiriza butumwa
Mugihe twabarungikira intumwa z’Imana zibiri barazi hakana natwe duca tubongereza inguvu tuba rungikira uwugira gatatu, bababwira bati:- mu vy’ukuri twebwe turungitswe kuri mwebwe
Nabo babishura bati:- mwebwe ntaco murimwo, atari uko muri mu bantu nkatwe, nayo nyene imigisha ntanakimwe yamanuye, mwebwe muri ababeshi gusa
Bavuze bati:- Umuremyi wacu niwe afise ubumenyi atamakenga arimwo yuko twebwe twarungitswe kuri mwebwe
Kandi ntakiri hejuru yacu atari ugushikana ubutumwa bw’Imana buri k’umugaragaro
Baca bavuga bati:- mu vy’ukuri twebwe ntitwumvikana kubera mwebwe nimutareka twebwe tuzoba tera iminana kandi izobashikira ivuye iwacu n’ibihano bibabaza cane
Bavuze bati:- ukutumvikana kwanyu mwebwe nyene, yo! kuko mwibutswa mugabo mwebwe muri mu bantu mwarenze akarimbi
Haciye haza umuntu ningoga na ningoga avuye kuruhande rwakure rw’ico gisagara avuga ati:- bantu banje nimukurikire izi ntumwa
Nimu bakurikire babigishe batarinze kubasaba impembo iyariyo yose, mugihe abo bantu bari mubarongotse
Nikuki ntosenga uwandemye, niwe ariho muzo subizwayo
Mbega jewe nkurikire izindi Mana atari Imana yonyene rudende, niyaba Imana ishaka kungirira inabi, ibisabisho vyabo ntaco bizomarira n’ikintu na kimwe kandi ntibazondokora
Ninagira gutyo nzoba ndimu bantu bazimiye mubuzimire buri k’umugaragaro
Ntankeka jewe ndemeye Umuremyi wanyu mugabo ndabasavye mu nyumvirize
Ababwira ati:- niwinjire mw’Ijuru, nawe yishura ati:- iyo abantu banje babimenya
Ingene Umuremyi wanje yangiriye ikigongwe nuku mpezagira, nkaba ndimu bahawe iteka ntangere
Ntitwa bamanuriye abantu biwe arizo ngabo zivuye mw’ijuru, inyuma yiwe kandi ntitwari mubazi manura
Ntacabaye atari akaruru kamwe nk’isase, bose baca bara zimangana
Vyari	kuba	ngombwa	mukuba	humuriza	abo	bantu	batashikiwe n’intumwa y’Imana n’imwe, mugabo bamye bijajurira gusa
Mbega ntibabona abantu isinzi twahoneje imbere yabo yuko batagaruka iwabo
Kandi nta muntu uwariwe wese atazo shengezwa imbere yacu
N’ikimenyetso	kiri	kuribo	n’Isi	yapfuye,	tuzoyizura	nugukura	muriyo imbuto bazohora bafungura
Tugira muriyo imirima hamwe n’ibiti vy’imitende n’imizabibu	hamwe nugu cishamwo amariba muriyo
Kugira ngo bafungure muri ivyo vyamwa, kandi n’amaboko yabo ntaco yakoze, mbega ntibashima
Hahayagizwa Imana yaremye ikigabo n’ikigore muri vyose muvyo Isi inagisha no mumitima yabo hamwe nivyo batazi
N’ijoro	n’ikimenyetso	kuribo	kuko	ariho	bakura	mwo	umurango, mumwanya bagaca baba mumwijima
N’izuba	rigenda	gushika	kugituro	caryo,	iryo	n’iteguro	ry’uwufise ububasha n’ubumenyi
N’ukwezi	twagupimiye	ibituro	vyakwo	kugeza	naho	gusubira	kuba gutoyi cane nk’igishishwa c’icamwa c’umutende gishaje cane
Ntazuba rishikira	Ukwezi canke Ijoro ngo rirenge Umutaga, mugabo vyose biguma birerembera munzira zavyo
N’ibimenyetso	kuribo	bimenyesha	yuko	twajanye	abavyeyi	babo mumato yari yuzuye mwo ibintu
Twabaremeye ivyo burira ko bimeze nkivyo bazo kurira ko
Nitwa shaka twoshobora kuba somesha nturi kandi ntamufasha azoba arimwo canke uwuzoba rokora
Atari kumpuhwe zivuye iwacu hamwe nukuba girira akamaro mukiringo kigufiya
Mugihe babwiwe bati:- nimutinye ibiri imbere yanyu hamwe n’ibiri inyuma yanyu kugira ngo muronke imihezagiro y’Imana
Ntakimenyetso icarico cose kibashikira mubimenyetso vy’Umuremyi wabo atari uko batavyitaho
Mugihe babwiwe bati:- nimutange muvyo Imana yabahaye, bamwe bahakanye Imana yabo y’ukuri baca babwira abemeye Imana yabo y’ukuri bati:- mbega tubarishe ibifungurwa mubo Imana yishakiye wenyene mwebwe ntimurimwo atari mubuzimire buri k’umugaragaro
Nabo bavuga bati:- iri sango rizoba ryari nimwaba muvugisha ukuri
Ntaco barindira atari ijwi rimwe gusa rizo sokora imitima yabo mugihe bazoba bariko baratongana aba nabariya
Kandi ntibazo shobora kuraga muri ico gihe canke ngo bashobore kugaruka ku bantu babo
Munyuma hazovuzwa inzamba, mukanya isase uzoca ubona bazutse bavuye muntatemwa zabo bagenda ningoga na ningoga bagenda ku Muremyi wabo
Bavuga bati:- yo! mbega ni nde yatuzuye muntatemwa zacu, ibi nivyo twemerewe nayene imigisha nivyo bavuze vy’ukuri intumwa z’Imana
Ntakizoba atari iborogo rimwe gusa, mukanya isase gusa bose bazoba bamaze gushengezwa imbere yacu
Uwo musi rero umutima w’umwumwe wese ntuzohemukirwa n’ikintu nakimwe, kandi ntimuzo rihwa impembo iyariyo yose atari kuvyo mwahora mugira
Mu vy’ukuri abantu bo mw’ijuru kuri uno musi bari mubikorwa vyabo biba nezereza
Abo	bantu	hamwe	n’imiryango	yabo	bari	mubitutu	begamiye kunyegamo z’iteka
Bazoronkerayo ivyamwa, kandi baronkereyo ivyo bipfuza mwo vyose
Amahoro	gusa	niryo	jambo	rizoba	rivuye	ku	Muremyi	wabo	nyene imigisha
Uno musi nimwi tandukanye nabo bantu babi
Mbega sinaba buriye mwebwe bantu yuko muto hirahira ngo musenge Shetani mu vy’ukuri n’umwansi wanyu ari k’umugaragaro
Yuko mwonsenga jewe Mana yanyu kuko ariyo nziza igororotse
Ntankeka Shetani yarazimije abantu benshi cane muri mwebwe mbega ico gihe nti mwiyumvira
Rero uwu niwo wamuriro udahera witiriwe Jahannamu mwamye mwemererwa n’Imana yanyu y’ukuri
Uno musi uri hejuru nimu winjire mwo kubera ubuhakanyi bwanyu
Kuri uwo musi tuzoziba iminwa yabo hanyuma amaboko yabo atuganirire ateko amaguru yabo abe ivyabona kuvyo bamye n’ivyemezo n’amaguru yabo abe kuvyo bahora bagira
Iyo dushaka twari kunogora amaso yabo bakaguma birukira mumayira, mugabo izo nzira bazibone gute
Iyo dushaka twari kubagira ibikoko ubwo nyene naho bari, rero ntibari gushobora kugenda iyo baja canke gusubira inyuma iyo bavuye
Nuwo duhaye ubuzima burebure tumusubiza inyuma mw’ishusho ryiwe ryambere, mbega ibi vyose ntibabishira mubwenge bwabo
Natwe ntitwa mwigishije amajambo y’ubuhizi kandi ntivyoba kuriwe, kandi ntiyari kuba iyi Qur’aani ntagatifu atari uko ari icibutso n’igitabu kigaragaza ibikenewe vyose k’umugaragaro
Kugira ngo atuze uwuri muzima muribo kandi hemezwe ijambo kubatemera Imana yabo y’ukuri
Mbega ntibabona yuko twebwe twabaremeye muvyo amaboko yacu yagize hamwe n’ibikoko batunze
Nivyo bikoko twarabi gamburukije rero murivyo birurirwa n’ibindi navyo biraribwa
No muri ivyo bikoko barabironkera mwo akamaro kenshi hamwe n’ibinyobwa, mbega nikuki badashima
Bagumanye	izindi	Mana	aho	kugumana	Imana	y’ukuri	kugira	ngo bafashwe nabo
Ntibashobora kubafasha nabo arizo ngabo zabo ziba cungereye
Rero ntibigutere agahinda kubera amajambo yabo, ntankeka twebwe dufise ubumenyi bw’ivyo banyegeza hamwe nivyo basemerera
Mbega	umuntu	ntazi	yuko	twamuremye	mw’Ima	ry’intanga?	none yabaye mukeba wacu ari k’umugaragaro
Yaradutangiyeko akarorero aribagira ukuremwa kwiwe aca avuga ati:- ni nde azozura amagufa y’abantu mugihe azoba yamaze kuvungagurika
Vuga uti:- uwuzo yazura nurya yayaremye ubwambere, nawe n’uwufise ubumenyi bwukurema ibiremwa vyose
Niyo yabagiriye umukomezwa uvuye mugiti kibisi mukaba kuri ico giti namwe mucatsako
Mbega uwaremye Amajuru n’Isi mbega ntabushobozi afise bwukurema nk’aba yaremye, kubera iki nawe ari Umuremyi mukuru nyene ubumenyi bw’ibintu vyose
Mu vy’ukuri itegeko ryiwe mugihe ishakiye ikintu icarico cose nukukibwira iti:- nube mumwanya isase kigaca kiba
Aninahazwa ry’uwufise muminwe yiwe harimwo ubwami bw’ibintu vyose, niwe niho muzo subizwayo mwese
Ndarahiye kubatonze imirongo n’iyindi
Kandi kuri barya batuza amabi yose
Kandi kuri barya basoma ubutumwa bw’Imana
Mu vy’ukuri Imana yanyu niyo yonyene gusa
Umuremyi	w’Amajuru	n’Isi	hamwe	nibimwo	hagati	yavyo	kandi n’Umuremyi w’ubuseruko bwose
Ntankeka twebwe twarasharije Ijuru riri hafi kw’isharizo ry’Inyenyeri
Nukuyi kingira n’amashetani yataye umurongo
Ntibashobore	kwumviriza	ibiremwa	vyeranda	no	mugihe	birukanywe kumpande zose
Bazoshirwa kure, kandi bazoba bafise n’ibihano bitazoba vako
Dukuye	mwo	uwusahuye	ikintu	gitoyi	munyuma	agaca	akurikiranwa n’igishirira gisayangana
Nimubabaze muti:- mbega nibo bafise ishusho rikomeye cane canke barya twaremye, ntankeka ni twebwe twabaremye tubakuye mw’ivu rimatanye n’irindi
Mbega uratangara nabo babifata minenerwe
Mugihe batujijwe ntiba gondozwa
Mugihe babonye ibitangaro vyacu babifata minenerwe
Nukuvuga	bati:-	ntivyari	kuba	ibi	vyose	atari	uko	ari	uburozi	buri k’umugaragaro
Mbega mugihe tuzosandaba nukuba ivu n’amagufa niko kuzoba ari ukuri kukuzurwa
N’abatama bacu bakera
Vuga uti:- egome muri ico gihe muzoba muri mubihano bitazoba vako
Iyo mumuriro udahera hazoba hari induru yurutavana ko munyuma yaho bazobona umuhero w’Isi washitse
Bazovuga bati:- yo! Uwu niwo wamusi w’impembo
Uwu niwo musi wugucibwa urubanza mwahora muhakana
Begeranye bamwe bahemukiye imitima yabo hamwe n’abagenzi babo hamwe nabo bahora basenga
Aho	gusenga	Imana	nimuba	rongore	munzira	yomu	muriro	udahera witiriwe Jahannamu
Nimuba hagarike mu vy’ukuri bazobazwa
Mufise iki ko mutarokorana
Kuri uwo musi bazoteterwa bimwe bitarabaho
Bazokwinjira babazanya bamwe n’abandi
Bavuga	bati:-	mu	vy’ukuri	mwebwe	mwamye	mudushikira	munzira z’ukuri
Nabo bishure bati:- ahubwo mwebwe bonyene ntimwari muba Isilamu
Ntabubasha twari dufise hejuru yanyu mugabo mwebwe nyene mwari mubataye umurongo w’ukuri
Rero intahe y’Umuremyi wacu iramaze gucibwa ntankeka tuzoyihonja
Nitwebwe bonyene twabatakaje tukaba twari mubantu bazimiye
Rero mu vy’ukuri kuri uwo musi bazoba bari mubihano bakoranijwe hamwe
Uku niko tuzogira abo bataye umurongo
Mugihe	bahora	babwirwa	yuko	atayindi	Mana	itegerezwa	gusengwa bimwe vy’ukuri atari Imana y’ukuri baguma banana
Nukuvuga bati:- yo! twebwe dusige Imana zacu kubera uyo ategura amajambo y’ubuhizi nawe ari umusazi
Ahubwo	yaje	afise	ukuri	nukwemeza	intumwa	z’Imana	zose	zabaye imbere yiwe
Mu vy’ukuri mwebwe ntankeka muzohonja ibihano bibabaza cane
Kandi ntimuzohembwa atari kuvyo mwahora mugira
Dukuyemwo abantu beranda b’Imana bagize ibikorwa vyabo vyiza
Abo bantu nibo bazoronka imigisha yabo bwite
Ivyamwa vy’ubwoko bwose kandi baterwe n’iteka ntangere
Mumirima y’imigisha myiza
Bari hejuru y’ubusaswa barabana n’abandi amaso kuyandi
Bakikuzwa n’ibirahuri birimwo ibinyobwa vyiza cane
Vyera derere bifise n’akanovera kuri abo bantu babinywera mwo
Kuri	ivyo	binywobwa	ntangorane	n’imwe	zizoba	zirimwo	canke ugutakaza ubwenge
Bazoba bari kumwe n’abapfasoni bafise amaso meza manini maniniya
Abo bapfasoni bameze nk’amagi yabitswe neza
Bazohura bamwe n’abandi babazanya
Hanyuma avuge umuvugizi umwe muribo ati:- mu vy’ukuri jewe nari mfise umugenzi
Uwahora ambwira ati:- mbega wewe uri muri bamwe bemera	Imana yabo y’ukuri
Yuko	mugihe	twebwe	tuzo	sandaba	nukuba	ivu	n’amagufa	mbega twebwe tuzorihwa
Nawe azovuga ati:- mbega muzo mu runguruka
Nawe azo runguruka aze amubone ari hagati y’umuriro udahera witiriwe Jahannamu
Hanyuma aze amubwire ati:- ndarahiye kw’izina ry’Imana wewe wari wegereje kunzimiza
Iyo	itaba	imigisha	y’Umuremyi	wanje	ntankeka	nari	kuba	mubo shengezwa n’ibihano vyo mumuriro udahera
Mbega na twebwe turi mu bantu bazo subira kwitaba Umuremyi wacu
Atari	urupfu	rwacu	rwaho	hambere	kandi	twebwe	ntituzo	subira guhanwa
Ntankeka iyi niyo ntsinzi niniya
Rero akarorero nkaka niko bogira abo bogira
Mbega ikaze nkiri siryiza, canke kuronka igiti citiriwe Zaqqum
Mu vy’ukuri twebwe twagize ico giti nk’igihano caba hemukiye imitima yabo
Mu	vy’ukuri	ico	n’igiti	kivuye	hagati	y’umuriro	udahera	witiriwe Jahannamu
Ivyamwa vy’ico giti bimeze nk’imitwe y’amashetani
Ntankeka bazofungura kuri ico giti no kurico buzuze inda zabo
Hanyuma ntankeka bazo shikirwa kubera uburure bw’ico giti n’uruvange rw’amazi y’amarike
Hanyuma mu vy’ukuri ingaruka yabo bantu yazoba ari ayo mumuriro udahera witiriwe Jahannamu
Mu vy’ukuri basanze abavyeyi babo barazimiye
Nabo nyene baca batwarwa nugukurikira ingendo zabo
Kandi ntankeka abantu benshi bakera barazimiye imbere yabo
Mu vy’ukuri twararungitse abagabisha kuri abo bantu
Rero nurabe uko yabaye amaherezo yabo bantu batujijwe
Atari abagamburutsi b’Imana bigiriye ibikorwa vyabo vyiza
Mu	vy’ukuri	intumwa	y’Imana	Nuhu	(iii)	yaraduteye	akamo, n’abamwitavye b’intungane tumeze gute twebwe
Twaramurokoye hamwe n’abantu biwe bari muvyago bihambaye
Twarahezagiye umuryango wiwe ngo babe aribo baguma kw’Isi
Duca tumusigira ku bantu baje munyuma yiwe
Amahoro y’intumwa y’Imana Nuhu (iii) asasagare kw’Isi yose
Mu vy’ukuri uku niko duhemba abagira ineza
Mu vy’ukuri yari mubantu bacu bemeye Imana yabo y’ukuri
Munyuma yaho niho twaca twibiza bamwe n’abandi
Mu vy’ukuri intumwa y’Imana Ibrahimu (III) yari mumurwi wiwe
Yarayikoreye idini y’Umuremyi wiwe n’umutima mwiza cane
Yaramubwiye	Se	wiwe	hamwe	n’abantu	biwe	ati:-	mbega	mwebwe musenga iki
Kuvyiyadukije gusa vy’amamana aho yobaye Imana y’ukuri, nizo Mana mwipfuza
None n’ibihe vyiyumviro vyanyu hejuru y’Umuremyi w’ibiremwa vyose
Hanyuma yaciye yitegereza mu kwitegereza kunyenyeri
Avuga ati:- mu vy’ukuri jewe ndarwaye
Nabo baramuretse gutyo baca bamuha ibitugu barigira
Nawe aca agenda mumpisho no ku Mana zabo azibwira ati:- mbega mufise iki ko muda fungura
Mubaye gute ko mutavuga
Hanyuma arahindukira abakubita n’ukuboko kwiwe kw’iburyo
Baca baza n’ingoga na ningoga
Aca ababwira ati:- oh! Mbega musenga muvyo mwibaziye kubwanyu n’amaboko yanyu
Mugihe Imana ariyo yabaremwye hamwe nivyo mugira vyose
Nabo	bishura	bati:-	nimu	mwubakire	inyubakwa	hanyuma	mu mujugunyire muri uwo mukomezwa
Rero bashatse kumu girira amarorerwa, mugabo duca	tuba girira kuba aribo badebukiwe
Nayo intumwa y’Imana Ibrahimu (iii) yababwiye iti:- jewe ndagiye ku Muremyi wanje niwe azondongora
Ewe Muremyi wanje, numpe mu bantu bagira ineza
Niho twamuha inkuru nziza y’ikibondo gitekanye
Mugihe yashika kurugero rw’ukugenda nukugaruka ari kumwe nawe niho yamubwira ati:- ewe kibondo canje, mu vy’ukuri jewe nabonye mundoto zanje yuko no kubaga, rero nawe niwiyumvire neza, none wewe ubibona gute? Nawe amwishura ati:- ewe data wanje nugire nk’uko wategetswe nanje uzonsanga Imana ibishatse ndimu bantu batenyenya
Bose hamwe uko ari babiri mugihe biyemeza imbere y’Imana nuguca amuryamika hasi kugira ngo amubage
Muri uwo mwanya isase twaciye tumu hamagara duti:- ewe ntumwa y’Imana Ibrahimu (iii)
Uramaze kwemeza yandoto yawe, mu vy’ukuri uku rero niko duhemba abagira neza bose
Ntankeka iri n’igeragezo riri k’umugaragaro
Rero duca dukabisha n’igikoko cukubarwa gifise iteka ntangere
Duca tumusigira kubaje munyuma yiwe
Amahoro y’Imana abe kuntumwa y’Imana Ibrahimu (iii)
Uku niko duhemba abantu bagira ineza bose
Ntankeka yari mubantu bacu bemeye Imana yabo y’ukuri
Hanyuma	twamuciriye	agace	yuko	azokwibaruka	intumwa	y’Imana Is’haqa (iii) n’intumwa muntumwa z’ abagira ineza
Duca turamu hezagira hamwe n’intumwa y’Imana Is’haqa (iii) hamwe no muruvyaro rwabo, kuko aribo babaye mubagira ineza. hamwe n’abahemukiye imitima yabo bimwe bigaragara
Mu vy’ukuri twebwe twarabagiriye impuhwe intumwa y’Imana Mussa (iii) hamwe n’intumwa y’Imana Haruna (iii)
Duca turaba rokora hamwe n’abantu babo mugihe bari mungorane zidasanzwe
Duca tubakingira nabo baca baba bene intsinzi nyakuri
Bose uko ari babiri twabahaye igitabu gitanga umuco
Duca turabarongora munzira igororotse
Hanyuma duca tubasigira mubaje munyuma yabo
Amahoro y’Imana abe kuntumwa y’Imana Mussa (iii) hamwe na Haruna (iii)
Ntankeka uku niko duhemba abagira ineza
Ntankeka bari mubantu bacu bemeye Imana yabo y’ukuri
Mu vy’ukuri, intumwa y’Imana Il’yaasiiyn (iii) yari muntumwa z’Imana
Mugihe yabwira abantu biwe ati:- mbega mwebwe ntimutinya
Mutabaza isanamu ryitwa Baa’la, mukareka gusaba umwiza wabaremyi
Imana	ariyo	muremyi	wanyu	n’Umuremyi	w’abavyeyi	banyu	baho hambere
Baramu hakanye ntankeka rero bazo shengezwa mubihano
Dukuyemwo abantu b’Imana basukuwe nayo nyene
Twamusigiye kubaje munyuma yiwe
Amahoro y’Imana abe kuntumwa y’Imana Il’yaasiiyn (iii)
Ntankeka uku niko duhemba abagira ineza
Mu vy’ukuri yari mubantu bacu bemera Imana yabo bimwe vy’ukuri
Mu vy’ukuri intumwa y’Imana Lutwi (iii) yari muntumwa z’Imana
Mugihe twamurokora hamwe n’abantu biwe bose
Dukuye mwo umukenyezi ashaje mubasigaye inyuma
Hanyuma niho twahonya abandi
Mu vy’ukuri mwama mubacako mugitondo
No mw’ijoro nyene, mbega mwebwe ntimutegera
Mu vy’ukuri intumwa y’Imana Yunusu (iii) yari muntumwa z’Imana
Mugihe yirukira mubwato bwikoreye ibintu vyinshi
Baca bagira amatora aca aba mubatsinzwe nuguca atabwa mumazi
Mukanya ifi ica iramumira mugihe yari muba taweko umwikomo
Iyo ataba yari mubantu basenga Imana yiwe y’ukuri
Ntankeka	yari	kuguma	munda	y’iyofi	kugeza	k’umusi	wizurwa ry’abantu bose
Mugabo	twaciye	tumujugunya	kunkengera	z’ikiyaga	nawe	aremvye cane
Duca tumu nagishiriza uruyuzi rw’itango yaguma afungura
Twaramutwaye ku bantu ibihumbi ijana n’abarenga
Baca baremera, nukuba nezereza kugeza kugihe caho basandabira
Nimu	babaze	muti:-	mbega	Umuremyi	wawe	niwe	afise	ibibondo vy’abigeme nabo bakaba bafise ibibomdo vy’abahungu
Mbega	twebwe	twaremye	Abamarayika	kuba	yuko	aribo	bakenyezi nabo bakaba ivyabona
Muragabe ku vyiyadukiza kuribo n’ivyo bavuga
Imana yaravyaye, mu vy’ukuri kuribo ntankeka n’ababeshi
Yoba yaratoye ibibondo vy’abigeme gusumba ibibondo vy’abahungu
Mubayeho gute! Muca urubanza gute
Yo! Mbega mwebwe aho muri ntimwibuka
Canke mwebwe murafise ivyemezo biri k’umugaragaro
Nimuzane igitabu canyu ni mwaba muvugisha ukuri
Nabo bashizeho imiryango hagati yabo n’ibisigo, n’ivyo bisigo vyari vyamaze kumenya yuko atankeka kuribo bazo shengezwa
Imana iri kure n’ingene bayihayagiza
Dukuye mwo abantu beranda batowe n’Imana
Rero ntankeka mwebwe hamwe nabo musenga
Ntimushobora kuba zimiza
Atari bamwe bazo kwinjira mu muriro udahera
Ntan’umwe muri twebwe atari uko afise ubwicaro bwiwe buzwi
Mu vy’ukuri muri twebwe harimwo abatonda ku mirongo
Hariho n’abandi muri twebwe bahayagiza Imana y’ukuri
Mu vy’ukuri bamye bavuga
Iyo tuba dufise igitabu nkuko babifise ba bantu baho hambere
Ntankeka twari kuba mu bantu beranda b’Imana bisukuye
Ico gitabu baragi hakanye rero ubu vuba bazomenya
Kandi ntankeka ijambo ryacu riramaze gushika ku bantu bacu bahawe ubutumwa
Yuko aribo bazo rokorwa
N’ingabo zacu nizo zizo tsinda
Rero nimu bareke kure mu mwanya mutoyi gusa
Kandi mu bitegereze gusa nabo ubu vuba bazobona
Yoh! barahimiriza ibihano vyacu
Rero mugihe bizo manuka kurubuga rwabo hazoba hari mugitondo kitari ciza ku bantu batujijwe
Nimu bareke mumwanya mutoyi gusa
Nurabe gusa, nabone ubu vuba bazobona
Umuremyi	wawe	ari	kure	nivyo,	Umuremyi	w’iteka	hamwe	n’ivyo bayihayagiza ko
N’amahoro y’Imana asasagare kuntumwa z’Imana zose
Nihayagizwa ryose ryiza niry’Imana, Umuremyi w’ibiremwa vyose
Swaad, (Insiguro y’iyi ndome hamwe n’uwufise ubumenyi bwayo bwose buzi Imana yonyene gusa). Ndarahiye kuri iyi Qur’aani ntagatifu ifise ubutumwa nyakuri
Mugabo abahakanye Umuremyi wabo bari mu bishima nugu higanwa
Twahoneje abantu bangahe imbere yabo, batako bakoma induru mugabo umwanya w’ukurokoka wamaze guhera
Baratangaye mugihe bashikirwa n’uwutuza ava muribo hanyuma abatemera Imana yabo y’ukuri bavuze bati:- uyo muntu n’umurozi kandi n’umubeshi
Yagize Imana zose kuba ari Imana imwe gusa, ntankeka iri n’ijambo ry’igitangaza
Baciye bitahira bamwe mubakuru babo bavuga bati:- nimwigire kandi mwigumanire n’izo Mana zanyu, mu vy’ukuri iri n’ijambo rikenewe
Twebwe ntitwigeze twumva ibi bintu yuko muri iyi migenzo yacu yanyuma, kandi ntivyamye ho ibi vyose atari uko ari ivyadutse gusa
Niwe wenyene yamanuriwe ubu butumire gusa natwe ntitwabuhabwa, mugabo abo bantu bari bafise amakenga gusa kubera ubutumire bwanje, ahubwo ntibara honja ibihano vyanje
Mbega barafise ububiko bw’imigisha y’Umuremyi wawe, nyene ubushobozi atanga vyose
Canke barafise ubwami bw’Amajuru n’Isi hamwe n’ibiri hagati yavyo, rero nibafate inzira ibashikana yo
Izi n’ingabo zizo gendeshwa ningoga muvyondo vy’abahakanyi vyagendeshejwe ningoga aho hambere
Abaho hambere barahakanye abantu bo kuntumwa y’Imana Nuhu (iii) nabo kuntumwa y’Imana Aadi (iii) na Fir’auni nyene amazu y’inkingi zikoma komeye
Na Thamuda hamwe n’abantu bokwa Lutwi n’abantu bo mukibira c’ibiti vyinshi iyo niyo mirwi yabo
Abo bose bara hakanye intumwa z’Imana, rero ibihano vyanje vyaraba shikiye
N’aba ntibarindira atari akaruru kamwe gusa kukuzurwa kwabo kata rindiriza
Bama bavuga bati:- Muremyi wacu, nutuzanire bimwe mubihano vyacu imbere yuwo musi wugu harurwa
Nutenyenye kuri ivyo bavuga, mugabo wibuke wa muntu wacu mweranda ariwe Daudi (iii) nyene inguvu, mu vy’ukuri yari umuntu agaruka ku Mana n’ubu gamburutsi
Mu vy’ukuri twebwe twara gamburukiye imisozi hamwe nawe ininahaze kuva k’umugoroba no mugitondo
Hamwe n’inyoni zegereranijwe hamwe n’izindi zose zara mugamburukira
Duca dushira mubwami bwiwe ubushobozi nukumuha ubumenyi bw’ugucira imanza abantu
Mbega warashikiwe n’inkuru z’abari mumatati baca basimbira mucumba c’intumwa y’Imana Daudi (iii)
Mugihe binjira kwa Daudi (iii) yarabatinye nabo baca bavuga bati:- ntutinye kuri twebwe turi mumatati, umwe muri twebwe yarahemukiye mugenzi wiwe, none nuducire urubanza rw’ukuri, kandi ntuhengame ahanaka kandi uturongore munzira igororotse
Mu vy’ukuri uyu ni mwene wanje, afise intama z’inyana mirongo icenda n’icenda, nanje nkaba mfise inyana imwe gusa mugabo yavuze ati ndamuhe iyi rwanje ayitungire, none yananiye mu majambo
Avuga ati:- ni vy’ukuri yaguhemukiye mukugusaba iyo ntungwa yawe mukwongereza kuntungwa ziwe, ntankeka abari mw’ishirahamwe benshi bama bahemukirana bamwe kubandi dukuyemwo abemeye Imana yabo y’ukuri nukugira ibikorwa vyiza, nabo bantu bari kurushi, mu mwanya intumwa y’Imana Daudi (iii) yabona yuko twamuhaye ikibazo, aca asaba ikigongwe ku Muremyi wiwe n’ugupfukama n’ubwitonzi ntangere nugu tumbera ku Muremyi wiwe
Duca tumugirira ikigongwe kuri ivyo vyose, mu vy’ukuri arafise kuri twebwe icubahiro kininiya n’ahantu heza
Ewe Daudi (iii) mu vy’ukuri twebwe twaguhaye ubutegetsi ng’aha kw’Isi, rero nubacire abo bantu urubanza rw’ukuri kandi ntukurikire ivyo umutima wawe ushatse ntuze ukuzimize munzira nziza y’Imana, mu vy’ukuri bamwe bazimira nuguta inzira y’Imana abo bantu bazoronka ibihano bikaze cane kubera ukwibagira kwabo wa musi wuguharurwa
Kandi twebwe ntitwaremye Amajuru n’Isi hamwe n’ibirimwo vyose kubusa gusa, ibi vyose nivyo bikeka bamwe batemera Imana yabo y’ukuri, rero ibihano bikaze cane vy’umuriro udahera bizoba shikira bamwe bahakana Imana yabo y’ukuri
Mbega tubagire bamwe bemeye Imana yabo y’ukuri nukugira ibikorwa vyiza yuko boba bangana n’abononyi bagira ubwo bwononyi ng’aha kw’Isi, canke tubagire aba gamburukira Imana ko bangana n’abononyi
Iki gitabu twakimanuye kuri wewe, kikaba gifise imihezagiro myinshi cane kugira ngo abantu bategere neza, iyumvire amajambo yaco hamwe n’abafise ubwenge nabo bategere neza
Twarahaye intumwa y’Imana Daudi (iii) ikibondo citwa Suleymanu (iii) akaba yari mu bantu beza, kandi akaba yari afise n’ubwitonzi ntangere
Mugihe bwagoroba yashikirijwe Ifarasi zihumuye zihagaze nazo zikaba zari zihwahutse mugihe zitegetswe kwiruka
Yaciye avuga ati:- jewe nkunda ibintu vyiza mukwibuka Umuremyi wanje, mu nyuma zafarasi zinyegeza inyuma y’uruzitiro
Nimu bagarure iwanje, hanyuma aca atangura kuzi hanagura kumaguru yazo no kumazosi yazo
Twaramuhaye intumwa y’Imana Suleymanu (iii) duca dushiraho uwundi mubiri hejuru y’inyegamo yiwe hanyuma aragaruka wenyene
Aca avuga ati:- Muremyi wanje, nungirire ikigongwe kandi umpe n’ubwami, kandi ntuze ubuhe uwariwe wese munyuma zanje, ntankeka ni wewe mutanzi wa vyose
Duca tumu gamburukiza umuyaga ugenda buhoro buhoro kw’itegeko ryiwe, naho ushaka gushika hose
Hamwe n’ibisigo n’abubatsi n’abibira mumazi
N’ibindi bisigo biboshwe n’iminyororo
Iyi n’ingabirano yacu twaguhaye tutarinze guharurirana, rero nuyitange canke uyigumye utarinze kugiriranira ibiharuro
Mu vy’ukuri arafise kuri twebwe icubahiro n’ahantu heza
Kandi mwibuke intumwa yacu y’Imana Ayyubu (iii) mugihe Umuremyi wiwe yamuhamagara avuga ati:- mu vy’ukuri Shetani yanshikirije ibishoboka hamwe n’ingorane
Ihute nuku kuguru kwawe, naya niyo mazi apfuse yukwisukira hamwe n’ayandi yukunywa
Duca tumuha abantu biwe hamwe n’abandi nkabo hamwe nabo kumigisha ivuye iwacu hamwe n’ubutumwa ku bantu bafise ubwenge
Nufate amasonga y’uduti mukuboko kwawe, hunyuma uce umukubitisha umucance wawe, kandi ntute indahiro yawe, ntankeka twebwe twamusanze ari mu bantu batekereje kandi n’intore, mu vy’ukuri yari muba gamburutsi bacane
Bibuke abantu bacu ariyo ntumwa yacu y’Imana Ibrahimu (iii) na Is’haqa n’intumwa y’Imana na Yaaqubu bari bafise ubushobozi n’ubwenge buhagije
Mu vy’ukuri twebwe twagutoye kuri ryajambo ryiza cane ryukwibuka umusi w’imperuka
Kandi ntankeka abamyeho imbere yacu, nabo nimu bantu beza batowe
Kandi mwibuke intumwa y’Imana Ismaaili (iii) hamwe n’intumwa y’Imana Al’yasaa (iii) n’intumwa y’Imana Dhul’qiflu (iii) n’abo bose bari mu bantu b’intungane
Ubu n’ubwibutso mu vy’ukuri abatinya Imana yabo y’ukuri igituro cabo caho bazo garukira hazoba heza cane
Imirima yukwicara mwo mubuzima bwabo bwose izoba yuguruye imiryango yayo kubera bo gusa
Bazo kwegamira kunyegamo basaba ivyamwa vyinshi hamwe n’ibinyobwa
Hamwe nabo bazoba ho n’abanega babo bahumurije amaso yabo kubatambukanyi babo
Ibi nivyo mwaraganiwe k’umusi w’imperuka
Mu vy’ukuri iyi niyo migisha yacu idahera
Nuko rero mu vy’ukuri bamwe barenga imbibe ingaruka zabo zizoba ziri ahantu habi cane
Wamuriro witiriwe Jahannamu niwo bazokwinjiramwo naho nahateguwe nabi cane
N’uku bizoba rero nibahonje amazi y’amarike n’amashira
N’ibindi bihano nk’ibi ni vyinshi
Izi nizo ngabo zizo kwinjira hamwe namwe, mugabo ntizaronse ahantu heza zishikira mugabo zizo kwinjira mu muriro udahera
Bavuze bati:- mwebwe ntakaze ryiza mufise mwebwe nimwe mwatumye turonka ibihano aho naho n’ahantu h’ubwicaro bubi cane
Bavuze bati:- Muremyi wacu, abatumye tugira ibi vyose, n’ubongereze ibihano vy’incuro zibiri iyo mu muriro udahera
Bazovuga	bati:-	vyabaye	gute	ko	tutababona	babantu	twahora tubaharura ko bari mu bantu babi
Erega twaraba kengereye mugabo amaso yacu ntiyababona gusa
Ntankeka ibi bintu vy’amatati y’abantu bo mumuriro udahera nay’ukuri
Vuga	uti:-	mu	vy’ukuri	jewe	nd’uwutuza	gusa,	kandi	ntayindi	Mana itegerezwa gusengwa atariyo yonyene rudende nyene ubushobozi
Umumenyi w’Amajuru n’Isi hamwe nibirimwo vyose nyene ubushobozi hamwe n’ikigongwe cinshi
Vuga uti:- izi n’inkuru zihambaye cane
Mutitayeho namba
Ntabumenyi nari mfise bw’ibiremwa bitagatifu mugihe batumvikana
Simbwirwa ikintu na kimwe kuri jewe atari uko nd’umuntu atuza abantu kandi mboneka
Umuremyi wawe mugihe yababwira Abamarayika ati:- mu vy’ukuri jewe nzorema umuntu ndamukuye mw’ivu
Ninarangiza kurema uyo muntu nukumu huhera umutima uvuye	kuri jewe, rero nimuce mumupfukamira nukumu gamburukira
Bara gamburutse Abamarayika bose uko bangana bose
Dukuyemwo uwitwa Ibilisi yishimye nukuba muba hakanyi b’Imana
Imana yamubwiye iti:- ewe Ibilisi, n’igiki cakubujje ku gamburukira uwo naremye ku maboko yanje, mbega winamuye canke wabaye mubantu bakuru
Nawe yishura ati:- jewe ndimwiza gusumba uyo waremye, kuko jewe wandemye unkuye mu muriro udahera, nawe umurema umukuye mw’ivu
Imana	ica	ivuga	iti:-	nuve	muri	uwo	muriro	udahera	kuko	uramaze gutabwa kure n’imigisha yanje
Mu vy’ukuri umuvumo wanje uzoba hejuru yawe kuri kugeza k’umusi w’imperuka
Nawe yishura ati:- Muremyi wanje, numpe umwanya na mutoyi gusa kugeza k’umusi bazozurwa ibiremwa vyose
Imana imubwira iti:- nivyo wewe uri mubaronse ikibanza c’ukubaho
Kugeza kumwanya w’umusi wategekanijwe
Nawe yishura ati:- ndarahiye k’ukuri kw’iteka ryawe ntankeka jewe abo bantu bawe nzobazimiza uko bangana bose
Dukuye mwo ba bantu bawe muribo ar’intore
Imana ivuga iti:- ndarahiye mvugishije ukuri
Mu vy’ukuri jewe nzokwuzuza mu muriro udahera kuri wewe Shetani hamwe n’abagu kurikira muribo
Vuga uti:- jewe sindaba saba impembo kuri ibi, kandi jewe sindi mu bantu bitegeka
Ntivyari kuba ibi vyose atari uko ari ubutumwa ku bantu bose
Kandi ntankeka mwebwe muzomenya inkuru ziwe mumwanya
Imanuka ry’iki gitabu gitagatifu nikivuye ku Mana nyene ubushobozi hamwe n’ubuhizi buhagije
Mu vy’ukuri twebwe twaku manuriye iki gitabu bimwe vy’ukuri, rero n’usenge Imana yawe nukuyigira yuko ariyo Muremyi wenyene gusa
Uwizerwa w’Umuremyi n’Imana yonyene gusa, mugabo bamwe bagira abandi kuba arizo Mana aho kuba ariyo yonyene rudende bavuga bati:- twebwe abo ntituba senga mugabo niba dushikane hafi cane y’Imana, mu vy’ukuri Imana izocira urubanza ruri hagati yabo kuvyo batumvikanye ko, ntankeka Imana ntirongora umubeshi w’umuhakanyi w’Imana
Iyo Imana ibishaka ngo ironke ikibondo ntankeka yari gutora uwo yishakiye mubo yiremeye, mugabo iri kure yivyo vyose kuko n’Imana imwe yonyene rudende igira ivyo yishakiye
Niyo yaremye Amajuru n’Isi bimwe vy’ukuri, ikaba ariyo yapfuse Ijoro hejuru y’Umutaga kandi ikaba ariyo yapfuse Umutaga hejuru y’Ijoro kandi ikaba ariyo yagamburukije Izuba n’Ukwezi vyose bikagira gusa kugihe categekanijwe, mumenye yuko ariyo nyene ubushobozi kandi ariyo nyene ikigongwe cinshi
Niyo yabaremye mu mutima umwe, hanyuma igira mugenziwe kuba nkawe nukuba manurira ibikoko umunani harimwo impfizi n’inyana, rero ibarema munda z’abavyeyi banyu mufise iremwa ritandukanye n’irindi, riri mumyijima itatu, iyo rero niyo Mana ariyo Muremyi wanyu, ubwami bwose ni rwiwe kandi ntawundi asengwa bimwe vy’ukuri atariyo yonyene gusa, none mwebwe muhindukizwa hehe
Ni mwaba muri ahakanyi b’Imana y’ukuri, Imana ntibakeneye mwebwe mugabo ntiyemera ubuhakanyi bw’abantu bayo beranda, rero nimwa shima ivyo nivyo biyinezereza kuko biba bivuye kuri mwebwe, n’uwikorera ntazo kwikorera itu ry’uwundi, hanyuma ingaruka yanyu niku Muremyi wanyu, niyo izoba bwira ivyo mwahora mugira, ntankeka niyo ifise ubumenyi bw’ibiri mubikiriza vyanyu
Mugihe umuntu ashikiwe n’ingorane yama atakambira Umuremyi wiwe nugu tumbera iwe, hanyuma imuhaye imigisha ivuye kuriyo, wa muntu aca yibagira kuvyo yahora imu hamagarira aho hambere hahise nukuyi gereranya n’ibindi bintu kugira ngo ibatakaze munzira yayo, wewe rero nuvuge uti:- nunezerwe kubera ubuhakanyi bwawe mukiringo gitoyi gusa kuko wewe uzoba uri mu bantu bo mumuriro udahera
Mbega agire amasengesho mumyanya y’ijoro nugupfukama hamwe nuguhagarara nugutinya uwo musi w’imperuka hamwe nukwizera imigisha y’Umuremyi wiwe, wewe vuga uti:- mbega boshobora kungana bamwe bafise ubumenyi nabamwe badafise ubumenyi, rero abikebura nibarya bafise ubwenge gusa
Vuga uti:- mwebwe bantu banje bemeye Imana y’ukuri, ni mutinye Umuremyi wanyu, bamwe bagira ineza iyariyo yose ng’aha kw’isi bazoronswa ivyiza	vyabo,	n’Isi	y’Imana	iragutse	cane,	kandi	ntankeka	abatenyenya bazoronswa impembo yabo batarinze kurimburirana n’Imana
Vuga uti:- mu vy’ukuri jewe nategetswe yuko nsenga Imana nukwizera yuko Umuremyi ariwe wenyene gusa
Kandi nategetswe ngombe ndimu bantu bambere biyemeje kuba ndi umu Isilamu
Vuga uti:- jewe ntinya ibihano vy’umusi mukuru mugihe no cumurira Umuremyi wanje
Vuga uti:- jewe nsenga Imana yanje nemeza yuko ariyo yonyene gusa kandi ariyo Mana
Rero mwebwe nimusenge muvyo mukunda bitari Imana, nawe nuvuge iti:- mu vy’ukuri abazo ronka uruhombo nibarya bataye imitima yabo muruhombo hamwe n’abantu babo k’umusi w’imperuka, ni murabe urwo nirwo ruhombo ruri k’umugaragaro
Hazoshirwa hejuru yabo ibicu vy’umuriro no munsi yabo hazobayo ibindi bicu, kuri ivyo rero Imana irabagabisha abantu bayo, namwe bantu banje nimutinye
Na bamwe batitaho mukugira amasengesho y’amasanamu nuku gamburukira Imana, inkuru nziza nirwabo rero nubahe inkuru nziza aba bantu banje
Nabumviriza amajambo bagakurikira ayafise akamaro kuribo abo bantu nibo Imana yarongoye, kandi nibo bafise ubwenge
Mbega uwategerejwe gucirirwa urubanza rw’ibihano, mbega woshobora kurokora uwuri mumuriro udahera
Mugabo aba gamburukiye Umuremyi wabo bazoronka amazu maremare agerekeranye kuyandi mazu maremare, munsi yayo mazu hazocamwo inzuzi, iyo niyo ndagano y’Imana, kuko Imana ntirenga kundagano yayo
Mbega ntubona yuko Imana yamanuye amazi iyakuye mubicu hanyuma iyacisha hasi, nukuba amasoko y’amazi ari mukuzimu, hanyuma inagisha ivyamwa vy’ubwoko butandukanye, rero uca ubona ivyo vyamwa vyumutse nuguhindura amabara y’umuhondo, hanyuma bigaca bitangura gucika gurika, ntankeka muri ibi vyose harimwo ivyibutso ku bantu bafise ubwenge
Mbega umuntu Imana yugururiye igikiriza ciwe nukwemera ubu Isilamu kandi akaba ari mumuco uvuye ku Muremyi wiwe, rero ibihano bikaze cane bizoshikira bamwe bafise imitima y’agatimatare batibuka Imana namba, aba kandi nibo bari mubuzimire buri k’umugaragaro
Imana yamanuye amajambo meza cane arico gitabu kirimwo amajambo ahuje n’ayandi kandi aguma asubirwamwo, urukoba rw’umubiri narwo rwama ruhinda agashitsi kuri barya batinya Umuremyi wabo, hanyuma urukoba rwabo narwo hamwe n’imitima yabo iguma ihwahutse mukwibuka Umuremyi wabo, ubwo nibwo burokoke bw’Imana, kuri ubwo burokoke irongora uwo yishakiye, kandi uwurekuriwe n’Imana yuko yazimiye, ntankundi rero uwo muntu ntawuzo murongora
Mbega uwuzoba akingiye amaso yiwe n’ibihano bibi vyo k’umusi w’imperuka nayo abahemukiye imitima yabo bazobwirwa bati:- nimuhonje kuvyo mwamuye
Abamyeho imbere yabo barahakanye, n’ibihano vyaraba shikiye bivuye ahantu batazi
Imana yaciye ibahonjesha ibimaramare mubuzima bwo ng’aha kw’Isi n’ibihano vyo k’umusi w’imperuka nivyo bininiya iyo bobimenya
Ntankeka abantu twaraberetse uburorero butagira uko bungana buri muri iki gitabu gitagatifu ca Qur’aani kugira ngo abantu bagume bibuka
Iyi Qur’aani ntagatifu yamanutse mururimi rw’icarabu itarimwo ibintu bihuvya kugira ngo bikingire
Imana ibatangirako uburorero bw’umuntu afise basebuja bari mumatati, n’uwundi muntu afise Sebuja wiwe umwe wenyene gusa, mbega ubona yuko bongana mubuzima bwabo n’ugushimira Imana, mugabo benshi muribo ntavyo bazi
Mu vy’ukuri wewe uzosandaba, nabo nyene bazosandaba
Hanyuma ntankeka muzo kwitwara k’umusi w’imperuka imbere y’Umuremyi wanyu
Ni nde yoba ari umuhemu yahemukiye umutima wiwe gusumba uwubeshera Imana nuguhakana ukuri kwama mugihe kwamushikiye, none simuri wa muriro udahera aribwo bwicaro bwabo bahakanyi b’Imana y’ukuri
Nuwazanye ukuri nuku kwemeza, abo bantu nibo bagamburukira Imana yabo
Bazoronka ivyo bipfuza vyose ku Muremyi wabo, iyo niyo mpembo yabakora ibikorwa vyiza
Kugira ngo Imana ibahana gurire amabi yabo yose bagize nukubariha impembo yabo kuvyiza bahora bagira
Mbega Imana ntihagiza umuntu wayo, kandi baragutera ubwoba kuri barya mutari kumwe nabo rero uwaciriwe urubanza n’Imana yuko atakara ntawundi muntu yomu rongora
Nuwo Imana yarongoye ntawu shobora kumutakaza, mbega Imana siyo nyene ubushobozi ishobora kwihorera
Ubajije uti :- mbega ni nde yaremye Amajuru n’Isi, ntankeka bazokwishura bavuga bati :- n’Imana, nawe nubishure uti :- mbega mwebwe mubona gute muri bamwe musaba atari Imana y’ukuri, yuko Imana ishatse kungirira inabi, mbega barashobora kunkurira izo ngorane ziwe, canke ishatse kumpezagira mbega nibo bashobora gukingira imigisha yayo ? wewe nuvuge uti :- jewe Imana irampagije ni kuriyo bizera abayizera
Vuga uti :- mwebwe bantu banje, ni mugire ibikorwa vyanyu mutekereje nanje nuko nyene ndiko ndakora, rero ubu vuba muzobimenya
Ninde azo shikirwa n’ibihano bizomu tetereza hamwe nibizo manukira kuriwe kandi bibandanya
Twebwe twakumanuriye iki gitabu gitagatifu ca Qur’aani kubera abantu bose, kandi kugira ngo uba sobanurire ukuri, rero uwuzo rongoka ni kukamaro k’umutima wiwe, nayo uwuzo takara azo takara ntankeka azoba atakaye k’uruhombo rw’umutima wiwe, na wewe nturi mu bantu baba cungera
Imana niyo yica imitima y’abantu kumwanya w’urupfu rwayo, n’iyindi mitima itarapfa iri mw’itiro ryayo, rero ica igumya ya mitima yandikiwe urupfu hanyuma igaca isubiriza yayindi kugeza kumwanya wagenewe, ntankeka muri ibi vyose hariho icirwa ku bantu biyumvira
Canke nibo bigiriye ababa sabira imbere y’Imana? Wewe nuvuge uti:- naho ata butegetsi bafise bw’ikintu na kimwe kandi ntabumenyi bafise
Vuge uti :- isabirwa ryose riri kw’itegeko ry’Imana kuko ariyo nyene ubwami bw’Amajuru n’Isi, hanyuma mwese muzo subizwa iwe
Mugihe havuzwe Imana yonyene rudende, imitima yabamwe batemera umusi w’imperuka ica ishavura, no mugihe havuzwe abatavuga rumwe nabo mumwanya uca ubona banezerewe
Vuga uti:- ewe Muremyi waremye Amajuru n’Isi, ufise ubumenyi bw’ibintu bitaboneka n’ibiboneka, ni wewe uzocira urubanza ruzoba ruri hagati y’abantu bawe kuvyo bahora batumvikana ko
Niba abahemukiye imitima yabo iyo boba bafise ibiri ng’aha kw’Isi n’ibindi nk’ivyo, ntankeka bari gutanga kugira ngo bikombore kubijanye n’ibihano bibi vy’umusi w’imperuka, kandi bizo garagazwa ku Mana kuvyo batari bizeye
Hazo bonekana amabi yabimwe bahora bagira, kandi bazo kikuzwa nivyo bahora bafata minenerwe
Ingorane ishikiye umuntu aca adusaba twebwe, hanyuma tumuhaye imigisha ivuye iwacu aca avuga ati:- ibi ndabihawe kubera ubumenyi bwanje none sivyo, ico n’ikibazo mugabo benshi muribo ntakintu na kimwe bazi
Barayavuze aya majambo abamyeho imbere yabo mugabo ntaco vyabamariye muvyo bahora bagira
Rero barahuye n’amabi yivyo bakoze, n’abahemukiye imitima yabo muri aba, ubu vuba nabone bazohura n’amabi bahora bagira, nabo s’abazo nanirana
Mbega ntibazi yuko Imana itanga imigisha yayo kuwo yishakiye nukwima uwo yishakiye, mu vy’ukuri muri ibi vyose harimwo ibintu vy’ugutegera ku bantu bemera Imana yabo y’ukuri
Vuga uti :- mwebwe bantu banje mwahemukiye imitima yanyu, ntimu debukirwe kumigisha y’Imana, ntankeka Imana yama igira ikigongwe kubicumuro vyose, mu vy’ukuri niyo ifise ikigongwe cinshi kandi niyo nyene impuhwe zihagije
Nimu garuke ku Muremyi wanyu kandi muyi gamburukire imbere yuko mushikirwa n’ibihano vy’Imana hanyuma ntimuzo ronka umufasha
Nimu kurikire ibintu vyiza muvya manuwe kuri mwebwe bivuye ku muremyi wanyu imbere yugu shikirwa n’ibihano bije giturumbuka namwe mutabizi
Ntuze uvuge umutima w’umuntu uti:- ewe maganya yanje kuvyo nagabanije kuruhande rw’Imana, mu vy’ukuri jewe nari mubantu bafata ibintu minenerwe
Canke niyavuga iti:- iyo Imana indongora, ntankeka nari kuba mu bantu batakambira Imana
Canke ikavuga mugihe ibonye ibihano:- iyo ndonka ingaruka nari kuba mubagira ineza
Ni vy’ukuri kandi ntankeka warashikiwe n’amajambo yanje uraya hakana k’umugaragaro nu kwishima hanyuma uca uba muba hakanyi b’Imana
No k’umusi w’imperuka uzoba bona bamwe babesheye Imana mumaso yabo hamaze kwirabura, mbega simu muriro udahera witiriwe Jahannamu ariho hazoba ubwicaro bwabamye bishima
N’Imana izoba rokora bamwe bayitinya kubera intsinzi yabo, kandi ntibazo korwako n’amabi canke ntibazo teterezwa
Imana niyo rurema rw’ibintu vyose kandi niyo mureretsi w’ibiri hejuru y’ibintu vyose
Impfunguruzo z’Amajuru n’Isi zose ziri ku Mana nabamwe bahakanye amajambo y’Imana abo nibo bari muruhombo runiniya
Vuga uti:- mbega muntegetse gusenga uwutari Imana mwabijuju mwe
Mu vy’ukuri wewe warugururiwe hamwe n’abari imbere yawe yuko niwa gereranya Imana n’ibindi bintu ntankeka ibikorwa vyawe bizoba bibaye ivy’impfagusa, kandi ningombwa uzoba uri mu bantu bari muruhombo
Ahubwo wewe n’usenge Imana yawe gusa kandi ube mu bantu bashima
Ntibasoneye Imana yabo bimwe bikwiye, no k’umusi w’imperuka Isi yose izoba iri muminwe yayo, n’Amajuru yose azo zingirwa mukuboko kwayo kw’iburyo, nayo ikaba itandukanye nuku gabanukirwa n’ikintu icarico cose, kandi niyo iri hejuru gusumba kuvyo bayi gereraniriza ko
Hazovuzwa inzamba hace havamwo imitima y’abantu bari mumajuru hamwe nabari kw’Isi dukuyemwo uwo Imana yikundiye, hanyuma hazovuzwa iyindi nzamba igira kabiri aho rero niho hazozuka ibiremwa vyose bagume barabana gusa
N’Isi izosa yangana k’umuco w’Umuremyi wayo, n’ibitabu vyose bizobikwa hanyuma hace hazanwa intumwa z’Imana n’ivyabona vyazo, hanyuma hazocibwa urubanza ruzoba ruri hagati yabo bimwe vy’ukuri, kandi ntibazo hemukirwa
N’umutima wu mw’umwe wese uzorihwa kuvyo wakoze nayo niyo ifise ubumenyi buhanitse bw’ivyo bagira vyose
N’abahakanye Imana yabo y’ukuri bazojanwa mumuriro udahera witiriwe Jahannamu bari imirwi n’iyindi kugeza naho bazoyishikira yugururwe imiryango yayo n’abacungereye uwo muriro bazobwirwa bati:- mbega ntimwashikiwe n’intumwa z’Imana ziri muri mwebwe ziba somera amajambo y’Umuremyi wanyu nukuba tuza kw’ihuriro ry’uwo musi wanyu, nabone bazovuga bati:- nukubera iki? mugabo ryaremejwe ijambo ry’ibihano rizoba kuri bamwe bahakanye Imana yabo y’ukuri
Hazovugwa hati:- ni mwinjire muri iyo myugariro y’uwo muriro udahera hanyuma muce mwicarayo, mugabo ubwo bwicaro bumeze gute, bwabo bantu bishima
N’abemeye Umuremyi wabo bimwe biboneka bazojanwa mw’ijuru bari imirwi n’iyindi kugeza naho bazoshikira imyugariro yaho yamaze kwugururwa naba cungereye bazoba bwira bati:- amahoro y’Imana abe kuri mwebwe, kandi ni munezerwe, kandi mwinjire ng’aha mw’ijuru mubeho muzima bwanyu bwose
Nabo bazovuga bati:- ihayagizwa ryose ni ry’Imana kuko ariyo iri mw’ijuru kandi ikaba ariyo yatwemereye indagano yayo hamwe nukudusigira ibisigi vy’Isi tuzokwicara muri iyo mirima aho dushaka hose, rero n’impembo nziza zimeze gute z’abagize ibikorwa vyiza
Uzobona Abamarayika bakikuza hambavu y’inyegamo y’Imana bahayagiza nugu himbaza Umuremyi wabo, hakazo cibwaho n’urubanza ruzoba hagati yabo rw’ukuri kandi hazovurwa hati:- amahayagizwa yose meza nay’Imana Umuremyi w’ibiremwa vyose
Ha, Miiym. (Insiguro yizi ndome hamwe nuwufise ubumenyi bwazo zose n’Imana yonyene gusa)
Ukumanurwa kw’iki gitabu gitagatifu c’Imana bivana n’Imana nyene ubushobozi n’ubumenyi buhagije
Niyo ihanagura ibicumuro nukwakira imbabazi z’abantu kandi irakaze cane muguhana kwayo, kandi niyo nyene ubutore, kandi ntayindi Mana isengwa bimwe vy’ukuri atariyo yonyene gusa, n’ingaruka yavyose iri kuriwe
Ntibaharira kumajambo y’Imana matagatifu atari abahakanye Imana yabo y’ukuri rero ntuhendwe nukugenda genda kwabo mubisagara
Abantu bo kuntumwa y’Imana Nuhu (iii) imbere yabo hamwe n’imirwi yabo munyuma yabo hamwe n’ayandi makungu barateguye umugambi w’amabi kuntumwa yabo y’Imana kugira ngo bayifate, hanyuma bayi gandagure, rero baraharira kubitajanye n’ukuri kugira ngo bahindure ukuri, kuri ivyo naciye ndabafata n’amaboko yanje, mbega ibihano vyanje vyari bimeze gute
Uku rero niko bashikiwe abo batemera Imana yabo y’ukuri kw’ijambo ry’Umuremyi wawe yuko ari abantu bo mumuriro udahera
Bamwe barerura inyegamo y’Imana y’iteka hamwe n’abayikikuje bose baninahaza Umuremyi wabo nukuyi takambira kandi barayemera bimwe vy’ukuri nababa sabira ikigongwe bemeye bimwe vy’ukuri bavuga bati:- Murenyi wacu ukwiye kubintu vyose no kumigisha yawe hamwe n’ubumenyi buhagije, nubagirire ikigongwe abo bantu bakigusavye ico kigongwe nugu kurikira inzira yawe kandi nuba kingire n’ibihano vyo mumuriro udahera witiriwe Jahannamu
Muremyi wacu, nubinjize mumirima yubudahera wabemereye, kandi ubahe n’ibi mubagize ivyiza mu bavyeyi babo hamwe n’abatambukanyi babo n’ibondo vyabo, ntankeka ni wewe nyene ubushobozi n’ubuhizi buhagije
Kandi ubakingire n’ivyago kuko uwo ukingiye n’ivyo vyago kuri uwo musi mu vy’ukuri wewe uzoba wamuhezagiye nuko rero iyo niyo ntsinzi niniya
Mu vy’ukuri bamwe bahakanye Imana yabo y’ukuri bazobwirwa bati:- ntankeka ukubanka kw’Imana ni kunini cane gusumba ukwiyanka kw’imitima yanyu mugihe mwahamagarwa ngo mube aba Isilamu b’ukuri namwe murahakana
Bazovuga bati:- Muremyi wacu, utwishe incuro zibiri usubira kutuzura izindi ncuro zibiri, rero natwe turemeye ibihano vyacu, mbega hari iyindi nzira yuguca mwo
Kubera yuko mugihe bahora bayivuga Imana yonyene gusa mwaca mwanka, mugabo igereranijwe n’ibindi bintu mwaca muvyemera, rero umucamanza wuno musi n’Imana iri hejuru yavyose kandi ariyo nkuru
Imana niyo izo bereka ibimenyetso vyayo hamwe nukuba manurira imigisha ivuye mw’ijuru, rero ntawibuka atari uwugarutse ku Mana yiwe
Rero ni muyisabe Imana, kandi muyigirire yo nyene ibisabisho vyanyu naho abo bahakanyi b’Imana yabo y’ukuri bazoshavura
Niyo nyene ubutegetsi buri hejuru cane, ikaba ishikiriza ubutumwa bw’amategeko kuwo yishakiye kubantu bayo beranda kugira ngo ubatuze k’umusi w’ihuriro ry’abantu bose
Umusi bazo bonekana imbere y’Imana, kandi ntankuru iyariyo yose izo kwinyegeza imbere y’Imana, no kuri uno musi ubwami bw’Imana buzoba ari ubwande? Nu bw’Imana wenyene rudende ariwe nyene ubushobozi buhagije
Uno musi umuntu wese azoronswa impembo yiwe kuvyo yakoreye ntawuzo hemukirwa uno musi, ntankeka Imana irafise umwete wuguharura
Nubatuze k’umusi uri hafi cane wugushika, mugihe imitima yabo izoba yamaze gushika kunkoratima nayo yuzuyemwo ibimaramare, rero abahemukiye imitima yabo ntabagenzi bazoba bafise canke uwuzoba sabira canke uwuzo gamburukirwa
Niyo ifise ubumenyi bw’ubuhemu bw’amaso yabo hamwe nivyo ibikiriza vyabo binyegeje
N’Imana yama ica urubanza rw’ukuri mugabo bamwe basenga ibitari Imana y’ukuri ntabuca manza bazoba bafise mu vy’ukuri Imana niyo yumva nuku bona
Mbega ntibagize ingendo zo ng’aha kw’Isi ngo bitegereze ingene yabaye impera n’imperuka y’ababaye ho imbere yabo? Bari bafise ubushobozi buhagije n’ububasha bukwiye ng’aha kw’Isi kubasumba n’Imana niyo yabashize mubiganza vyayo kubera ibicumuro vyabo, kandi ntibari bafise uwubakingira n’Imana
Ivyo nuko bahora bashikirwa n’intumwa z’Imana zifise n’ivyemezo biri k’umugaragaro mugabo barabahakanye ari naho Imana yabahanye, ntankeka niyo nyene ububasha, kandi niyo ikaze cane muguhana
Mu vy’ukuri twararungitse intumwa y’Imana Mussa (iii) hamwe n’ibitangaro vyacu hamwe n’ivyemezo biri k’umugaragaro
Nokwa Fir’auni hamwe no kwa Hamana na Qaaruni nibo baciye bavuga bati:- uwo muntu n’umurozi kandi n’umubeshi karuhariwe
Mugihe yabashikiriza ukuri kwama kuje kuva iwacu baciye bavuga bati:- nimugandagure ibibondo vy’abahungu vyose hamwe nabamwemeye bose hanyuma muze musigaze abakanyezi babo gusa nayo ingeso z’abatemera Imana yabo y’ukuri ntiziba atari uko vyama ari ivyimpfagusa
Fir’auni yavuze ati:- ni mundeke ndamu gandagure uyo Mussa (iii) hanyuma ace ahamagara Umuremyi wiwe amukingire, jewe Fir’auni ndafise amakenga yuko atazo kwonona idini ryanyu, canke ntaze kuzana umudugararo ngaha kw’Isi
Intumwa y’Imana Mussa (iii) imwishura iti:- jewe ndikinze ku Muremyi wanje hamwe n’Umuremyi wanyu aze ankingire n’umuntu uwariwe wese yishima kandi atemera umusi uhambaye wuguhanwa
Haca havuga umwe mu bantu baba Isilamu ati:- nawe akaba yari mu bantu bo kwa Fir’auni yanyegeza ubu Isilamu bwiwe ati:- Yoh! Mbega mugomba mwice umuntu ngo n’uko yavuze Umuremyi wanje, n’iyo Mana, mu vy’ukuri uyo muntu yaje kuri mwebwe afise n’ivyemezo biri k’umugaragaro akaba yaje ava ku Muremyi wanyu, rero niyaba ari umubeshi ubwo bubeshi bwiwe buri kuri we wenyene, kandi niyaba ari umunyakuri mwebwe muzoshikirwa na bimwe muri ivyo yabaraganiye, ntankeka rero Imana ntiyigera irongora uwurenga akarimbi, kandi akaba n’umubeshi karuhariwe
Mwebwe bantu banje, kuri uno musi murafise ubwami kandi murafise n’intsinzi ng’aha kw’Isi, none ni nde azo dufasha nuku turokora n’ibihano vy’Imana bidushikiriye? Fir’auni yishuye avuga ati:- ntakuntu noba hanura atari nkuko jewe ndabibona, canke jewe sindaba rongora atari munzira nziza yabarokotse
N’umwe muri bamwe bemeye Imana yiwe y’ukuri yagumye avuga ati:- mwa bantu banje mu vy’ukuri jewe ndabatinya nk’akarorero k’umusi w’imirwi y’abansi b’Imana
Nk’akarorero k’abantu b’intumwa y’Imana Nuhu (iii) hamwe n’abantu b’intumwa y’Imana Aadi (iii) n’intumwa y’Imana Thamuda (iii) hamwe nabaje munyuma yabo, n’Imana, rero Imana ntikunda uwuhemukira abantu bayo
Namwe bantu banje mu vy’ukuri jewe ndabatinyira kuri wa musi wugu hamagarana
Mugihe muzo hindukira inyuma, nta muntu azoba kingira ku Mana izoba ihari, nuwuzo ciribwa urubanza n’Imana yuko ari mu bantu bazimiye, uyo muntu ntawuzo murongora mu bantu uwariwe wese
Kandi ntankeka kera mwarashikiwe n’intumwa y’Imana Yussufu (iii) ifise n’ivyemezo biri k’umugaragaro, mugabo mwebwe mwabandanije mugira amakenga kuvyo yabashikirije, kugeza aho yasandaba niho mwaciye muvuga muti:- Imana ntizosubira kuzana iyindi ntumwa y’Imana munyuma yiwe, niba ari uko Imana yama ireka umuntu akazimira kuwarenze imbibe zayo no kubera ibicumuro vyuwitera amakenga
Abaharira kumajambo y’Imana badafise ivyemezo ivyarivyo vyose vyabashikiye, n’ishavuzo rihambaye imbere y’Imana n’imbere yabemeye Imana y’ukuri, uku niko Imana itera ikidodo kumutima yabiha yagiza nukwishima
Na Fir’auni yavuze ati:- ewe Hamana, nunyubakire ikimenyetso kugira ngo nshobore gushikira inzira
Inzira yo mw’ijuru kugira ngo mbone Imana ya Mussa (iii), mu vy’ukuri ndamuzi neza yuko ari umubeshi karuhariwe, uko rero niko Fir’auni yasharijwe kumabi y’ibikorwa vyiwe nukuzitirirwa inzira mugabo ingeso za Fir’auni ntizabaye atari uguhonywa kwiwe gusa
Numwe yemera yabandanije avuga ati:- bantu banje nimu nkurikire jewe nzoba rongora munzira y’ihumure
Mwebwe bantu banje, mu vy’ukuri ubu buzima bwo kuri iy’Isi n’umunezero gusa, kandi ntankeka niyo mw’Ijuru niyo nzu yukuba mwo burundu
Umugizi w’inabi ntaco azorihwa atari ibikwiranye n’amabi yiwe, n’uwugira ineza haba k’umugabo canke k’umugore nawe ari umu Isilamu, rero abo bantu bazo kwinjizwa mw’Ijuru baze bahabwe muri ayo majuru batarinze kugirirwa ibiharuro
Namwe bantu banje, ni kuki jewe ndaba hamagarira k’uburokoke namwe muka mpamagarira mumuriro udahera
Mumpamagaye ngo mpakane Imana nukuyi gereranya nuwo ntazi, nanje ndaba hamagarira k’uwufise ubushobozi kandi ariwe nyene imbabazi zihagije
Ntankeka mwebwe mumpamagaye ngo ngende gusenga abadafise ubutumwa bwo ng’aha kw’Isi canke ubutumwa canke ubwo mw’Ijuru n’ingaruka yatwese ni ku Mana, nabarenga imbibe z’Imana abo nibo bantu bo mumuriro udahera
Ubu vuba muzoyibuka kuvyo nababwiye, nanje ndabikesheje Imana ivyanje vyose, mu vy’ukuri irababona abantu biwe bose
Hanyuma Imana yaramukingiye n’amabi y’ingeso zabo bagize hamwe n’ibihano bibi vyabakikuje abo bantu bokwa Fir’auni nawe arimwo
Ibihano vyo mumuriro udahera bizo kwerekanwa mugitondo no kumugoroba no kuri uwo musi niho hazobonekera umusi w’imperuka haze hazovurwe hati:- nimu binjize abo bantu ba Fir’auni mubihano bikaze cane
Nibagira ibihari muri uwo muriro udahera mugihe abati shoboye bazoba bwira abamye bishima bati:- mu vy’ukuri twebwe twari mumurwi wanyu, mbega mwoshobora kudukurira igice gitoyi c’uwo muriro udahera
Bazovuga bamwe bahora bishima bati:- twese dukoraniye ng’aha Imana iramaze kuducira urubanza ruri hagati y’ibiremwa vyiwe
Nabazoba bari mumuriro udahera bazobwira abacungereye umuriro udahera witiriwe Jahannamu bati :- nimusabe Umuremyi wanyu atugabanirize umusi umwe w’ibi bihano
Bazobishura bati:- mbega ntimwamye mushikirwa n’intumwa z’Imana zanyu zifise ivyemezo biri k’umugaragaro, nabo bazobishura bati:- nukubera iki? nabo bazo babwira bati:- nimusabe n’ibisabisho vy’abatemera Imana yabo y’ukuri ntibibaho atari ubuzimire bw’impfagusa
Mu vy’ukuri twebwe dukingira intumwa z’Imana zacu hamwe n’abemeye mubuzima bwo ng’aha kw’Isi n’igihe hazohagarara ivyabona bizo kwemeza ibikorwa vy’ibiremwa vyose
N’umusi utazo fasha abahemukiye imitima yabo kuvyitwazo vyabo kandi bakazoronka n’umuvumo w’Imana, n’ubwicaro bwabo buzoba ari bubi cane
Mu vy’ukuri twarahaye intumwa y’Imana Mussa (iii) uburongozi dutako tubaha n’ibisigi bene Israeri igitabu c’Imana
Uburongozi hamwe n’icibutso ku bantu bafise ubwenge
Rero nimu tenyenye ntankeka indagano z’Imana ni z’ukuri na wewe nusabe ikigongwe kubera ibicumuro vyawe, uteko uhayagize Umuremyi wawe nukuyibuka uko bugorovye no mugitondo
Mu vy’ukuri bamwe bagira ibihari kumajambo y’Imana matagatifu atavyemezo bafise vyabashikiye ntabiri mumishaha yabo atari ubwishime gusa, mugabo ntaco bazoshikako ahubwo wewe niwikingire ku Muremyi wawe, mu vy’ukuri Imana niyo yumva nukubona
Mu vy’ukuri iremwa ry’Amajuru n’Isi ni rininiya cane gusumba iremwa ry’abantu bose, mugabo abantu benshi ntavyo bazi
Impumyi hamwe n’uwubona ntibangana, n’abemeye Imana yabo y’ukuri nukugira ibikorwa vyiza hamwe nabagira amabi y’amarorerwa mugabo muvyo mwibuka mwebwe bantu n’ibintu bikeyi cane
Mu vy’ukuri umuhero w’Isi uzoshika kandi ntamakenga arimwo, mugabo abantu benshi ntavyo bemera
